Left rail unified (matching widths + green top accent on pin button when doc pinned). Empty-state cards use AccentCard pattern (green / indigo / amber accents). **Forward-looking rule**: when a Phase X ship gets founder pushback on one specific element, do surgical rework preserving what worked + fixing what didn't — NOT a full re-revert. Diff-of-the-diff awareness keeps velocity.

## Platform-page consolidation sweep (locked 2026-05-09 evening — Phases A through E)

**The cleanup**: 14 sidebar entries → 9. Three orphaned routes deleted. One thin-wrapper route folded into a sibling tab as a properly redesigned section. Two heavy pages (decision-log + AI Copilot) refactored, not just resurfaced. The pre-sweep state had drift accumulated from rapid feature shipping; this is the refinement-mode discipline catching up.

**Phase A — kill dead surfaces** (3 routes deleted + 308 redirects in [next.config.ts](next.config.ts)):

- **/dashboard/playbooks** (735 lines) — orphaned. The CRUD UI for "pre-configured analysis templates" was never wired into the analyze pipeline; the `DecisionScorecard` + `ActOnThisPanel` components that referenced playbooks were not mounted in any production surface. Deleted the page route, the `/api/playbooks/*` route tree, the `src/lib/playbooks/{suggest,templates}.ts` library, and both orphan components. 308 redirect to `/dashboard/decisions`.
- **/dashboard/provenance** (315 lines) — duplicate. Read-only DPR archive duplicated the per-document export button on `/documents/[id]` + the per-container export on `/dashboard/decisions/[id]`. No new insights surfaced. Deleted the page + the orphaned `/api/provenance/route.ts`. 308 redirect to `/dashboard/decisions`.
- **/dashboard/cognitive-audits/effectiveness** (512 lines) — duplicate metrics. Avg quality + nudge feedback + quality trend already render on Analytics → Performance + summary cards on /decision-log. Deleted; 308 redirect to `/dashboard/analytics?view=performance`.

**Phase B — fold Decision DNA into Analytics → Intelligence with proper redesign**. The /dashboard/decision-dna route was a thin 26-line wrapper around `DecisionDNAPageContent`. Conceptually it's a personal-calibration surface, structurally identical to Bias Genome contribution / Decision Intelligence / Explainability already living on the Intelligence tab. **Refactor moves**: (a) `DecisionDNAPageContent` lost its self-styled `<h1>` + page-container styling — it's now a content component, not a page; the Analytics section heading provides the H1. (b) Three early-return branches (loading skeleton / error / empty state) all stripped of `className="container"` so they render cleanly inside Analytics. (c) Refresh button kept (right-aligned in a slim row) so the user can still re-fetch their calibration. (d) Section anchor `id="dna"` with `scrollMarginTop: 80` so /dashboard/analytics?view=intelligence#dna lands directly on the section. (e) Standalone /dashboard/decision-dna route + loading.tsx deleted; 308 redirect; sidebar entry removed; CommandPalette entry redirected; DecisionDNAPreviewCard deep-links updated.

**Phase D — refactor /decision-log** ([page.tsx](<src/app/(platform)/dashboard/decision-log/page.tsx>)). Was 1,086 lines with three structural problems: (1) duplicate 4-stat AuditSummaryCards rendering metrics already on Analytics, (2) inline collapsible "New Entry" form stealing real estate above the filter strip, (3) two stacked filter UIs (source chips row + status segmented control row). **Refactor moves**: (a) `AuditSummaryCards` deleted entirely. (b) New entry form lifted to a proper modal triggered by "+ Log entry" button — composer-grade input experience, doesn't push the feed down when opened. (c) Source filter chips + status segmented control collapsed into one filter row using `justifyContent: 'space-between'` + flex-wrap (~40px tall vs the prior ~80px). (d) Active source chip restyled with accent-primary border (was muted gray; now matches the rest of the platform palette). (e) Header buttons relabeled "Log entry" + "Submit audit" (action-first, sentence case). (f) Removed unused `motion` / `AnimatePresence` imports. The link to /effectiveness was dropped in Phase A. Now 1,040 lines; UX impact is much larger than the line-count delta.

**Phase E — refactor AI Copilot** (the founder-flagged miss). The /dashboard/ask page had a slogan-style "Your AI advisory team" hero that didn't communicate what the surface DOES, plus a confusing 3-state flow (empty → prompt-input intermediate → chat) with dual CTAs ("+ New Decision" sidebar button + "+ New Decision Session" hero button) that meant the same thing. **Refactor moves**: (a) Page-level header chrome removed — the [page.tsx](<src/app/(platform)/dashboard/ask/page.tsx>) is now a thin shell, header lives inside CopilotPageContent. (b) Intermediate prompt-input mode REMOVED (the "What decision are you working on?" detour). (c) Single composer-first empty state: small Sparkles eyebrow + "Ask, audit, or stress-test a decision." H1 + 3-line description + autofocus textarea with placeholder + ↵ to start hint + 4 role-tuned starter chips below. (d) Composer ALWAYS visible — typing + Enter IS the start-a-session action; ChatGPT/Claude.ai pattern. (e) Pinned-document chips moved from a dangling bottom strip into a contextual "Pin a document for grounded Q&A" row that only appears when no doc is pinned. (f) Sidebar's "+ New Decision" button now clears the active session so the composer surfaces ready for the next prompt (was previously routing to the redundant prompt-input mode). (g) `STARTER_DECISION_QUESTIONS` constant removed (only consumed by the deleted prompt-input mode). (h) `kbdStyle` const added for the keyboard-shortcut hints in the composer.

**Phase C — surgical /dashboard home cleanup**. Dropped `JournalWidget` mount + import — redundant with the unified `/dashboard/decision-log` feed (which already merges journal entries + cognitive audits into one surface). The dashboard widget added noise without new signal; the sidebar surfaces /decision-log one click away. The remaining widget stack (DecisionTriageWidget / NudgeWidget / ContainersWidget / OnboardingGuide) carries distinct action-driving signals.

**Resulting sidebar (14 → 9 entries)**:

  Dashboard

**Forward-looking rule**: when a future audit identifies a sidebar entry as a thin-wrapper-around-a-content-component, the right move is NOT to delete the route silently — it's to fold the component as a SECTION on a sibling page (with a proper redesign that strips its self-page chrome) AND add a 308 redirect from the old URL. The Decision DNA fold is the canonical pattern. When a sidebar entry is a duplicate of per-decision functionality (the Provenance archive vs. per-document/per-container DPR export), delete the route + redirect to the canonical surface; don't fold what doesn't add value.

## Phase G — Decision Log fold into Decisions (locked 2026-05-10 morning)

**The fold**: Decision Log was a standalone sidebar entry at `/dashboard/decision-log` rendering a unified journal + cognitive-audits feed. Founder pushback 2026-05-10 morning — "still too much cognitive load with all the pages — is the Decision Log really a necessary standalone page, can't we just incorporate elements from it into the Decisions page". Conceptually correct: journal entries + cognitive audits + DecisionContainers are all decisions, just at different levels of formality.

**Resulting structure on `/dashboard/decisions`**: three views accessible from one parent page via a `?view` query param + a 3-button view switcher in the page header.

- **Kanban** (default, no query param): workflow-grade containers (investment / acquisition / strategic) — daily-ops triage board.
- **Log** (`?view=log`): chronological feed of journal entries + cognitive audits. Powered by [DecisionLogFeed](src/components/decisions/DecisionLogFeed.tsx) — extracted from the deleted standalone page; accepts a `forwardRef` handle so the parent's "+ Log entry" button can trigger the modal.
- **Constellation** (sibling page at `/dashboard/decisions/constellation`): cognitive lineage between containers. Heavy SVG; justifies its own URL.

**Files deleted**: `/dashboard/decision-log/page.tsx` (1,040 lines).

**Redirect added**: `/dashboard/decision-log` → `/dashboard/decisions?view=log` (308 permanent).

**Sidebar (8 entries → 7)**:

```text
ACT: Dashboard / Decisions / AI Copilot
REFLECT: Analytics / Decision Graph (sub-nav) / Outcome Flywheel (sub-nav)
TOGETHER: Meetings & Rooms / Team / Settings
```

**Cross-references updated**:

- CommandPalette `decision-log` entry → renamed to `decisions-log`, routes to `/dashboard/decisions?view=log`
- `NotFoundContent.tsx` quick-link href updated
- `TimelinePhaseScrub.tsx` (2 hrefs) updated
- `founder-context.ts` Decision Log Unification + Cognitive Audits entries updated
- `dashboard/page.tsx` JournalWidget-removal comment updated

**Forward-looking rule**: when collapsing a sibling page into a parent's view-switcher pattern, prefer the `?view=X` query-param approach over a child route — it keeps the sibling URLs clean (the parent stays at `/parent`, the view stays at `/parent?view=Y`) and makes the view switcher a single component without route-level branching. Sub-routes (like `/dashboard/cognitive-audits/submit` or `/dashboard/decisions/[id]`) stay live; only the umbrella surface collapses.

## AccentCard primitive + visual-distinction discipline (locked 2026-05-09 evening — founder audit follow-up)

**The pattern**: every platform surface that stacks ≥3 cards in a column gets a top accent stripe per card so semantic role becomes visible at a glance. The founder flagged 2026-05-09 evening as "too many white cards with no visual distinction tightly packed" — the all-`.card` flat-white pattern was the recurring drift class across Settings, AI Copilot empty state, decision-log new-entry stack, and any tab with multiple sections.

**The primitive**: [src/components/ui/AccentCard.tsx](src/components/ui/AccentCard.tsx) — small wrapper with an `accent` prop (`'primary' | 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'danger' | 'muted'`). Each accent maps to a CSS variable for the top stripe, plus optional `tinted` flag for a subtle background blend (used on Danger Zone). Optional `title` slot for the icon + heading row.

**Semantic role mapping** (apply consistently across platform surfaces):

- **primary** (green) — primary actions, the lead/hero card on a tab (Account Information, Notification Preferences)
- **info** (indigo) — informational / data / export / preference surfaces (Display Preferences, Export your data, Slack workspace)
- **success** (green-tinted) — verified state / "all good" status (Security with 2FA + encryption checks)
- **warning** (amber) — contextual nudges, low-stakes attention (Product Tour replay, Pin-a-document hint on /ask)
- **danger** (red, often `tinted`) — destructive zones (Delete account, force-push warnings)
- **muted** (gray) — neutral / informational with no semantic colour

**Surfaces migrated 2026-05-09 evening (initial batch)**: Settings → Account tab (5 cards) + Preferences tab (2 cards) + Integrations tab (Slack workspace card). AI Copilot empty state composer + starter chips + pinned-doc hint. Each migration drops the `.card` className in favour of `<AccentCard accent="..." title={...}>`.

**Surfaces migrated 2026-05-09 evening (Phase F batch 2)**: Dashboard widget stack — DecisionTriageWidget (`accent="danger"`, also fixed dark-theme Tailwind drift), NudgeWidget (`accent="warning"`), ContainersWidget (`accent="primary"`). Settings sub-components — EmailForwardingSection (`accent="info"`), PersonaManager (`accent="warning"`). AccentCard primitive extended with `bodyStyle` prop for full-bleed row content (used by DecisionTriageWidget + NudgeWidget where rows carry their own padding).

**Surfaces migrated 2026-05-09 evening (Phase F batch 3)**: Dashboard KPI grid — 4 hero cards each with metric-coded accents (Total Documents indigo, Analyzed green, Avg Quality DYNAMICALLY grade-coded by value, Decision IQ primary green). Inline `borderTop` instead of full AccentCard wrap to preserve the existing `.stat-card liquid-glass-premium` look. Decision DNA Preview Card (3 render states: loading skeleton + discovery + populated, all `accent="primary"` since DNA is the proprietary calibration moat). Compliance page FrameworkCard with new `certStatusToAccent()` helper mapping `attested` → success / `targeted` → warning / `self_assessed` → info — a CISO scanning the Compliance tab now reads cert posture at a glance via the top stripe.

**AccentCard migration audit (locked 2026-05-13 — U-6 ship)**: Settings + Dashboard AccentCard migration is now COMPLETE. The only bare `<div className="card">` remaining in either directory is [InlinePasteMemoCard](src/components/dashboard/InlinePasteMemoCard.tsx) which uses an intentional LEFT-bar treatment (`borderLeft: '3px solid var(--accent-primary)'`) to visually distinguish from the AccentCard family's TOP-bar pattern. Documented as an intentional exception — future audits should not re-flag. **InsightsPageContent AccentCard migration — SHIPPED 2026-05-15.** The genuine semantic targets were migrated with per-content accents: the 4-tile trend stat-row (Avg Score→primary, Avg Noise→danger, Total Biases→warning, Analyses→success — the canonical metric-coded stat-row pattern), the full-page fetch-error card → danger, the market-intelligence error overlay → danger, the market-intelligence success card → success. **Intentional carve-outs (do NOT re-flag — these are the lock's "bare .card fine for one-off surfaces" class):** (a) the `[0,1,2,3].map` loading skeletons — a skeleton asserts no semantic role; a coloured stripe on a shimmer placeholder is wrong; (b) the Bias-Network viz-internal `.card` — it sits in the ANALYSIS-MATRIX grid-3 row whose siblings render their own viz components, so an accent there breaks row consistency, not solves indistinctness; (c) the risk-signal list-item that already carries a severity-coded `borderLeft` (same intentional LEFT-bar exception class as InlinePasteMemoCard — AccentCard's TOP-stripe would be a mixed metaphor); (d) the `card card-glow animate-slide-up` section wrappers — NOT bare; they're a deliberate glow + staggered-entrance pattern with their own visual distinction. **Dashboard remaining bare `.card`:** Activity-Feed collapsible section migrated → AccentCard info. The Documents section (`#documents` anchor, ~250-line deep-nested block with its own prominent search/filter header) + the transient upload-progress card + the document-list `.map` items + the already-green-tinted callout stay bare on purpose — anchored/transient/list-item/already-distinct, all the lock's carve-out class; close-tag rematch on the Documents block is pure regression risk for a marginal stripe on an already-highly-distinct section. **AccentCard primitive gained an optional `id` passthrough** so a future anchored bare-`.card` migration can't silently drop a fragment link (the bug class that would have hit `#documents`). The InlinePasteMemoCard LEFT-bar exception note above still stands.

**Forward-looking rule**: when adding a new card to ANY platform surface that stacks ≥3 cards, default to AccentCard with a deliberate accent choice. Falling back to bare `<div className="card">` is fine for one-off surfaces but any tab / page with ≥3 cards stacked MUST use AccentCard so the eye has visual hierarchy. When a new accent semantic is needed (e.g. a "calibration" colour), extend `ACCENT_COLORS` in AccentCard.tsx + document the new mapping here in the same commit.

## 3-Layer Positioning Frame (locked 2026-05-09 evening — Gemini-pushback validation)

**Architectural vocabulary** for cold investor conversations + pitch-deck slide 2 + senior-direct corp dev applications. Lifted from the 2026-05-09 Gemini-pushback validation pass; sharper than the prior CLAUDE.md positioning frame because it gives the reader a clean architectural slot for DI:

> **Snowflake owns data integrity. Salesforce owns execution discipline. Decision Intel owns the reasoning layer between them — the audit moment before capital is committed.**

Three layers, three primary questions, three categories of incumbent:

1. **Data integrity** (Snowflake / Databricks / BigQuery) — _"Is the data we feed into the call correct?"_ Mature category, multi-billion-dollar incumbents.
2. **Reasoning quality** (Decision Intel) — _"Was the call defensible at the moment of commit?"_ The audit moment before capital is committed. R²F + 22-bias taxonomy + 143-case library + 19-framework regulatory map + Brier 0.258. **The wedge.**
3. **Execution discipline** (Salesforce / Workday / NetSuite) — _"Did the decision actually get implemented?"_ Mature category, dominant incumbents.

**Use rules:**

- **The 3-layer frame is the OPENING LINE for cold investor calls + cold corp-dev applications.** Then bridge to the locked H1: _"The reasoning audit platform — R²F over a 22-bias taxonomy, scored as a Decision Quality Index."_ The 3-layer frame earns the reader's attention; the H1 is the category claim once they're listening.
- **Never the H1.** Per CLAUDE.md vocabulary lock the H1 stays _"Decision Intel is the reasoning audit platform."_ The 3-layer frame is supporting architectural vocabulary, not a replacement.
- **Never use the broader "system of record where core data is stored"** framing. That competes with Notion / Confluence / Drive (`company knowledge base` is in `BANNED_VOCABULARY` for this exact reason). The locked narrowing is _"system of record for DECISIONS specifically."_ The 3-layer frame is compatible with this — DI's "reasoning layer" is the decisions-specific narrowing.

**Where this lives in the codebase:**

- `src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/ThreeLayerModel.tsx` — interactive 3-layer visualization on the Path to $100M ARR tab. The opening-line copy is rendered there for the founder's recall.
- `src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/AiNativeMatrix.tsx` — Fragile Wrapper vs DI matrix with DI's specific moats in every cell (R²F + 22-bias + 143-case + 19-framework + Brier 0.258 + agentic-shift defense + Pan-African coverage + per-org Brier accumulation). Use when an investor or partner asks _"won't GPT-N+1 just do this?"_ The columns are the answer.

**Forward-looking rule:** when a moat changes (new framework added · new bias shipped · methodology version bump · new HXC persona), update the matching cell in `AiNativeMatrix.tsx` in lockstep. The matrix is procurement-grade differentiation only as long as every cell stays citable to a CLAUDE.md lock.

## M&A Workflow Native (P1 lock 2026-05-09 — capability sharpening, NOT positioning narrowing)

**The hybrid pivot direction (locked 2026-05-09 after the 2026-05-08 NotebookLM hybrid-path synthesis):** keep DI broad-positioning (4 HXC personas including fractional CSO; H1 stays "Decision Intel is the reasoning audit platform"), but harden the product into M&A-workflow-native shape. Three of four HXC personas are M&A-primary (mid-market corp dev / smaller-fund GP / PE-backed founder); the deepest product capability + the strongest career-credential overlap with M&A workflow specifically. The hybrid lets DI serve all 4 HXC personas without abandoning the broad positioning AND positions the founder for senior-direct corp dev hiring (per the 2026-05-09 NotebookLM senior-direct-path synthesis: technical-strategist track at Lazard / KKR Capstone / Vista Operating Group / Databricks / Snowflake via acqui-hire-structured deal terms, not analyst-track entry).

**13 named toxic patterns** (was 10) in `src/lib/learning/toxic-combinations.ts` `NAMED_PATTERNS`. The 3 M&A-specific patterns added 2026-05-09:

- **The Synergy Mirage** (overconfidence_bias + planning_fallacy with high monetary stakes) — the canonical M&A failure mode (70-90% of acquisitions fail to realize projected synergies per McKinsey + KPMG). Fires when synergy claims lack a NAMED OPERATIONAL MECHANISM + NAMED ACCOUNTABLE EXECUTIVE + MEASURABLE 90-DAY MILESTONE per BCG integration-best-practices. Severity Critical when synergies drive >25% of deal valuation; High when 10-25%; Medium when <10%. Revenue synergies flagged harder than cost synergies (30-50% vs 60-80% realization rates).
- **The Conglomerate Fallacy** (illusion_of_validity + halo_effect) — far-adjacency acquisition justified primarily by target's growth or brand momentum rather than core operational overlap or "why us as parent" thesis (Porter parenting advantage). Anchor failures: Bed Bath & Beyond + Container Store, AOL + Time Warner, Daimler + Chrysler.
- **The Winner's Curse** (anchoring_bias + overconfidence_bias) — auction-dynamic language driving bids above intrinsic value. Fires on "preempting competitor B" / "strategic necessity" / "competitive process" / "we cannot let X get this asset." Required context: monetaryStakes='high' AND timePressure=true. WeWork S-1, Quibi, post-2010 SPAC wave anchors.

Plus M&A-specific framing layered into existing **Sunk Ship** (deal-escalation language: "we have already spent $X on diligence and advisor fees"; Lockheed Martin reach-forward losses anchor) + **Yes Committee** (rubber-stamp justification of CEO/sponsor's pet acquisition with zero documented dissent; Microsoft-Nokia $249B-evaporation anchor).

**3 new M&A document subtypes** in `src/lib/prompts/investment-vertical.ts` `INVESTMENT_DOCUMENT_TYPES` (was 6, now 9): `qofe` (Quality of Earnings — flag for adjusted-EBITDA inflation + run-rate normalization + customer-concentration disclosure), `synergy_model` (synergy projection spreadsheet — fires Synergy Mirage hardest), `integration_plan` (post-merger integration plan — cultural divergence + IT-simplicity fallacy + talent-flight + customer-concentration + synergy ownership + Day-1 operating model). Plus `ic_memo` + `cim` `DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS` sharpened with the 5 named M&A toxic combinations + Porter "why us as parent" question + Seller-Halo Filter framing.

**Cascade discipline when adding new toxic combinations:** (a) `NAMED_PATTERNS` array in `src/lib/learning/toxic-combinations.ts`, (b) `BIAS_DETECTIVE_PROMPT` TOXIC COMBINATIONS section in `src/lib/agents/prompts.ts`, (c) all required bias keys must exist in `BIAS_EDUCATION` (verify before adding), (d) Education Room flashcard in `src/components/founder-hub/education/education-room-data.ts` cognitive_biases deck. The 4-part cascade is the same shape as adding a new bias to the 22-bias taxonomy.

**Cascade discipline when adding new document subtypes:** (a) `INVESTMENT_DOCUMENT_TYPES` array, (b) entry in `DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS` dict, (c) optional entry in `STAGE_BIAS_OVERLAYS` if stage-specific risks exist. The Document.documentType field is free-text in Prisma — no schema migration needed.

**M&A marketing surfaces + case-tagging cascade (extended 2026-05-09 alongside the P1 ship):** the public `/bias-genome` + `/how-it-works` + case-study cards must surface the new M&A patterns (otherwise a Head of Corp Dev / PE Deal Partner reading the marketing-side moat explanation sees zero M&A vocabulary and the cascade discipline lives only in the internal pipeline). Six marketing-side data structures updated: (a) `src/lib/data/bias-genome-seed.ts` `TOXIC_PAIR_DEFS` extended with Synergy Mirage / Conglomerate Fallacy / Winner's Curse — feeds `/bias-genome` page + `/how-it-works` toxic combinations section. (b) `src/components/marketing/genome/ToxicNetworkGraph.tsx` `PATTERN_COLORS` extended with 3 new edge colours (violet-500 / cyan-600 / rose-700). (c) `src/components/marketing/genome/GenomeMethodologyViz.tsx` mitigation-step rows swap one general-decision pattern for Synergy Mirage so the canonical M&A failure mode lands in the methodology viz. (d-e) `src/components/marketing/CaseStudyBiasGraph.tsx` + `CaseStudyBiasGraph3DCanvas.tsx` `TOXIC_PAIRS` extended in lockstep so the case-card biases-web renders M&A-pattern edges correctly. (f) `src/app/(marketing)/case-studies/[slug]/page.tsx` `TOXIC_DESCRIPTIONS` extended so the detail-page chips render plain-language descriptions. **Case-tagging — 14 anchor cases retro-tagged across two ship batches**: First batch (with the marketing-data-cascade ship): WeWork (`+ Winner's Curse`), Quibi (`+ Winner's Curse`), HP-Autonomy (`+ Winner's Curse + Synergy Mirage`), AOL Time Warner (`+ Synergy Mirage + Conglomerate Fallacy`), Yahoo-Tumblr (`+ Winner's Curse`), Bed Bath & Beyond (`+ Conglomerate Fallacy`), Sears Holdings (`+ Conglomerate Fallacy`). Second batch (deeper M&A failure-library coverage): Microsoft-Nokia (`+ Synergy Mirage + Conglomerate Fallacy`), Myspace News Corp (`+ Conglomerate Fallacy`), Steinhoff (`+ Conglomerate Fallacy`), Carillion (`+ Conglomerate Fallacy`), GE financial-conglomerate (`+ Conglomerate Fallacy`), GE-Alstom (`+ Synergy Mirage + Winner's Curse`), WorldCom (`+ Synergy Mirage + Conglomerate Fallacy`). **Skipped** (reviewed but pattern doesn't fit): Toshiba + HBOS (CEO-pressure / branch-level fraud, not M&A-driven), JC Penney (pricing strategy not adjacency), Yahoo (rejection of Microsoft offer is seller-side, our patterns are buyer-side), Theranos / Magic Leap / MoviePass (funding-round dynamics, Winner's Curse stays M&A-strict). Without these tags `bias-genome-seed.ts` `caseCount` for the new patterns would render as zero on `/bias-genome`. **Forward-looking rule**: when a new M&A toxic combination ships in `NAMED_PATTERNS`, the SAME commit must update (i) the 6 marketing-side data structures above, (ii) at least 1-3 retro-tagged anchor cases in the 143-case library, otherwise the marketing surface either fails to render the pattern or renders it with no case examples. The full cascade is now 10 surfaces (4 internal pipeline + 6 marketing data structures + ≥1 case-tagging) — same lockstep discipline as the bias-taxonomy cascade.

**M&A workflow surfacing on public pages (extended 2026-05-09 — second marketing pass after the data-cascade ship):** the data cascade ensured the 3 new patterns RENDER correctly; this pass makes M&A workflow nativeness VISIBLE. Two surfaces: (i) `/bias-genome` gains a dedicated **M&A Pattern Coverage** section between Toxic Combinations and Biological-State Signals — new component `src/components/marketing/genome/MnaPatternCoverage.tsx` renders a procurement-grade stat strip (70-90% McKinsey + KPMG synergy-miss rate, 9 M&A artefact types, 5 toxic combos, EU AI Act Art. 14 hook) plus a 3-column pattern grid where each column shows the named pattern + bias pair + mechanism explanation + every anchor case from the 143-case library tagged with that pattern (sorted recent-first, links to case detail). A Head of Corp Dev / PE Deal Partner sees "here are 14 deals you've heard of, audited against our 3 M&A patterns" — converts the M&A claim from theoretical to procurement-grade. (ii) `/how-it-works` gains a **Section 4b — M&A workflow overlays** between Toxic Combinations (Section 4) and DQI (Section 5) — shows the 5-stage deal lifecycle (Sourcing → Diligence → IC Review → Closing → PMI) with each stage carrying its document types + pattern coverage + audit detail + status (live vs roadmap). Stage 5 PMI is honestly marked `roadmap` per the CLAUDE.md M&A roadmap (PMI overlays are backlog post-acqui-hire); Stages 1-4 are `live` because pattern detection already fires at the appropriate stage based on document type, even though deal-stage UI overlays are scheduled for P3 / acqui-hire window. **Forward-looking rule**: when adding new deal-stage overlays or M&A patterns, the same lockstep applies — surface them on `/bias-genome` MnaPatternCoverage + `/how-it-works` Section 4b in the same commit. Marketing visibility lives downstream of code visibility; if the marketing page lags the engine by even one sprint, the procurement-grade authority signal degrades.

**DQI explainability panel — SHIPPED 2026-05-09 evening (4-commit batch f86143f → this commit).** Founder ask delivered end-to-end: clickable DQI score on every audit opens a dynamic visualization showing what the score is made of, what computed at every place, and how every element in the document influenced each weighted component. Built FROM THE BUYER'S SEAT (Head of Corp Dev / PE Deal Partner / GP / fractional CSO) — no jargon, no internal stat names, plain language at every layer.

**Architecture (4 commits)**:

(1) `f86143f` — Data layer. Extended `DQIComponent.breakdownItems` population from compoundRisk only to all 7 components: biasLoad (one item per detected bias, formatted name like "Anchoring Bias (critical)" with verbatim memo excerpt), noiseLevel (judge-count + average-score + disagreement-spread rows), evidenceQuality (verified / contradicted / unverifiable buckets), processMaturity (5 hygiene check rows + System 1/2 dominance row when material), complianceRisk (frameworks-checked + violations rows), historicalAlignment (failure-pattern-matches + success-pattern-matches + amplifier rows). Added optional `excerpt?: string` to `DQIInput.biases` so verbatim memo excerpts flow through. Helper `formatBiasNameInline` keeps snake_case out of buyer-facing labels. 10 new vitest tests lock buyer-language discipline (no snake_case, no "jaccard", explicit "potential — not legal determinations" qualifier on compliance violations).

(2) `45cd4d4` — UI component. New `src/components/dqi/DqiBreakdownPanel.tsx`. Modal dialog rendered when DQI badge is clicked. Header carries overall score + grade band ("Workable — material gaps to close before committee" replaces "C grade"). 7 component cards each with: plain-language displayName ("Cognitive biases detected" not "biasLoad", "Reasoning consistency" not "noiseLevel", "Decision process" not "Process maturity", "Regulatory exposure" not "Compliance risk", "Historical pattern match" not "Historical alignment", "Compound failure patterns" not "compoundRisk"), 1-line plain-language description, severity-coloured score, "Contributes X% to your score" weight in plain words, click-to-expand breakdown with per-element rows showing label + signed impact + evidence (verbatim memo passage where present) + "What to do" call-out when score < 60. Methodology footer in plain language ("Same memo audited again will produce the same score — no judgment calls in the math") — explains determinism without saying "deterministic."

(3) `273d611` — Wiring on `/documents/[id]`. OverviewTab DQI card now wrapped in `<button onClick={openPanel}>` with "Click to see how it's computed →" affordance hint. DQIData type alias upgraded to full `DQIResult` so the panel reads breakdownItems on every component. `<DqiBreakdownPanel>` mounted as sibling of the clickable card.

(4) This commit — Memory consolidation. CLAUDE.md NEXT-SHIP marker flipped to SHIPPED. founder-context.ts coaching block updated.

**Deliberately deferred (scope discipline)**:

- Post-upload reveal on `/dashboard` InlineAnalysisResultCard: the wow-moment animation shouldn't be slowed by a panel-fetch; the existing "Deep Dive →" link routes to /documents/[id] where the panel is live.
- Deal page composite DQI breakdown on DealCompositeHero: the composite is an average of per-doc scores — different shape than the per-audit panel. The deal page already has IcReadinessGate (Gate 6 surfaces critical patterns) + per-document DQI cards link to /documents/[id]. Deal-level composite breakdown is a separate ship that would aggregate breakdownItems across multiple docs.

Add a matching `COMPONENT_META` entry in DqiBreakdownPanel.tsx with displayName + description + icon + actionHint. The data layer + UI layer move in lockstep — never ship a component without buyer-facing copy.

**DQI explainability panel — extended to 3 audit-landing surfaces (locked 2026-05-09 evening, surfaces 2 + 3 of the founder ask).** The 4-commit DQI Explainability ship above (f86143f → ccec8ab) wired the panel onto `/documents/[id]` only. Two follow-up surfaces ship together so the breakdown is reachable from every audit-landing moment in the product:

(2) **Post-upload reveal on `/dashboard`** ([InlineAnalysisResultCard](src/components/analysis/InlineAnalysisResultCard.tsx)). The score column is now a clickable button that lazy-fetches the full `DQIResult` from `/api/dqi?analysisId=X` on first click and opens `DqiBreakdownPanel`. Lazy-fetch keeps the wow-moment reveal fast (the user pays the ~200-400ms only when they actually want the breakdown). The dialog only opens AFTER the fetch resolves so there's no empty-modal flash; until then the affordance hint reads "Loading breakdown…" instead of "Click to see how it's computed →". Same panel component as the document-detail surface — single buyer-facing language source. Disabled when `analysisId` is null (rare race condition where the SSE completion event hasn't yet supplied the analysis row id).

(3) **Deal page composite breakdown on `/dashboard/deals/[id]`** ([DealCompositeHero](src/components/deals/DealCompositeHero.tsx) + new [DealDqiBreakdownPanel](src/components/dqi/DealDqiBreakdownPanel.tsx)). Different shape from the per-audit panel — the composite is the simple average of per-document scores, so the right decomposition is "where did this composite come from" (per-document rows + cross-document recurring patterns), NOT "which weighted component contributed what" (that's the per-doc panel, one click away). Sections in order: (a) per-document rows sorted worst-first with score + grade + click-through to `/documents/[id]` so the reader drills into the lowest-scoring artefact in one click; (b) recurring biases across the deal with affected-doc counts; (c) compound failure patterns (Synergy Mirage / Conglomerate Fallacy / Winner's Curse / etc.) with severity + doc counts; (d) cross-document conflicts strip when the deal has crossRefFindings — surfaced with high-severity emphasis. Only the composite-DQI block is clickable, not the bias signature strip (that's already a flat surface). Backwards-compat: the click-to-open requires `dealName + documents` props; older callers (kanban preview cards) that don't pass these get the prior non-clickable layout. **Architecture rationale**: composite is a NAVIGATION SURFACE not a decomposition surface. Decomposition lives on the per-doc audit; deal-level navigation routes the buyer to the right per-doc audit in one click. This avoids the trap of duplicating per-component breakdown at two levels (which would require N+1 DQI fetches at deal-page load and would diverge from per-audit numbers when methodology versions bump).

**Forward-looking rule**: when a new audit-landing surface ships, default to mounting `DqiBreakdownPanel` (per-audit) or `DealDqiBreakdownPanel` (composite) based on whether the score is a single-doc DQI or an averaged composite. Both panels read from the canonical `DQIResult` / `DealAggregationDto` shapes — never invent a third panel for a new surface; pick one and feed it the right data.

**M&A hard-layer ship · Proposal 4 — synergyValidationNode pipeline node (locked 2026-05-09 evening).** Added a first-class deterministic pipeline node for synergy_model audits. Bumps the pipeline from 12 nodes (8 parallel after intelligenceGatherer + 4 sequential) to 13 nodes. Reads `state.parsedStructuredData` (set at audit-start time from Document.parsedStructuredData per Proposal 1), runs `summariseSynergyDefensibility` (pure function, no LLM call, milliseconds), writes `state.synergyDefensibility` for downstream consumers. **Architectural value-add over the prior text-extraction path**: (1) deterministic — same input → same output, procurement-defensible code path that's reviewable line-by-line vs LLM judgment buried in biasDetective; (2) first-class state — synergyDefensibility becomes a state field downstream nodes (metaJudge especially) can consume alongside their LLM signals; (3) pipeline observability — pattern detection happens in a NAMED PIPELINE NODE that shows up in the lineage on the DPR's pipeline manifest and the analyze-stream progress events. **State annotations added to graph.ts**: `parsedStructuredData?: unknown` (read from Document at audit-start), `synergyDefensibility?: unknown` (written by synergyValidationNode). Both annotated with last-write-wins reducers + null defaults. **AuditState (types.ts)** mirrored. **Graph topology**: synergyValidationNode added as 8th parallel node after intelligenceGatherer (was 7); fan-in to metaJudgeNode unchanged shape, just one more edge. **Skip semantics**: when documentType !== 'synergy_model' OR parsedStructuredData absent, the node returns no state mutation — downstream sees synergyDefensibility: null and behaves identically to the legacy path. **Pipeline progress**: analyze-stream NODE_LABELS gains the 13th entry "Synergy Validation". **No DQI weight changes, no DPR shape changes, no Prisma migration** — Proposal 4 is purely additive on top of Proposals 1+5 (Prisma fields) and 3 (DQI 7th component). **Forward-looking rule**: when adding new type-aware deterministic nodes (qofeValidationNode, integrationPlanValidationNode, etc.), follow the same shape — read from parsedStructuredData via kind discriminator, write to a dedicated state field, register in graph.ts as parallel-after-intelligenceGatherer, add to NODE_LABELS for progress UI.

**M&A hard-layer ship · Proposal 3 — DQI 7th component compoundRisk + methodology 2.2.0 (locked 2026-05-09 evening).** Added a 7th weighted component to the DQI scoring engine that directly penalises named toxic combinations. Previously compound patterns affected DQI INDIRECTLY through the constituent biases; now they show up as a first-class line item in the score with a transparent severity-driven penalty. **Weight rebalancing**: `WEIGHTS.biasLoad` dropped from 0.28 → 0.22 to make room; new `WEIGHTS.compoundRisk: 0.06`. All 7 weights still sum to 1.0. **Severity penalties**: critical -25, high -12, medium -5, low -1, base 100, floor at 0. **Methodology version trichotomy** (`METHODOLOGY_VERSION = '2.2.0'`, plus exported `METHODOLOGY_VERSION_2_1_0 = '2.1.0'` + `METHODOLOGY_VERSION_LEGACY = '2.0.0-no-validity'`): audits with `compoundPatterns` supplied → 2.2.0; with validity but no compound → 2.1.0; with neither → 2.0.0-no-validity. Each DQIResult carries the stamp so procurement readers can tell which methodology produced any given score. **breakdownItems on DQIComponent**: new optional field `Array<{label, impact, evidence?}>` carrying per-pattern impact data — designed for the upcoming clickable DQI explainability panel ship (founder ask 2026-05-09 — show users exactly how the score is composed and which document elements influenced each weighted component). compoundRisk component populates breakdownItems with one entry per pattern, sorted worst-first, ready for direct UI consumption. **Platform-baseline stability**: new `SYNTHETIC_WEIGHTS_LEGACY_2_0_0` constant pins `computeSyntheticDQI` + `computeBrierFairPredictedDqi` to the original 2.0.0-seed weights (biasLoad 0.28, etc.) so the platform-baseline Brier (0.258) stays stable when live WEIGHTS rebalance. Live audits advance with methodology versions; calibration baselines stay fixed at the version they were computed under. **Wired through three DQI routes**: `/api/dqi`, `/api/v1/dqi`, `/api/explainability/[analysisId]` all fetch `analysis.toxicCombinations` and pass `compoundPatterns` into `computeDQI`. Schema-drift fallback: legacy ToxicCombination rows with null severity → severity derived from toxicScore at the route boundary. **Forward-looking rule**: when adding a new DQI component, follow the same shape — extend WEIGHTS (rebalance + sum to 1.0); extend DQIInput with optional input field; extend DQIResult.components; populate breakdownItems for the explainability panel; bump METHODOLOGY_VERSION + add a new stamp constant for the prior version; pin synthetic functions if the change would shift the platform-baseline Brier.

**M&A hard-layer ship · Proposal 2 — server-side namedPatterns aggregation (locked 2026-05-09 evening).** Replaced the client-side toxic-combination detection in IcReadinessGate (the stopgap from the cascade-depth audit) with a canonical server-side aggregation. `AnalyzedDocument` interface gained optional `toxicCombinations: Array<{patternLabel, severity, toxicScore}>` field. `aggregateAnalyses()` groups by patternLabel, aggregates documentCount + topSeverity (max across docs) + maxToxicScore, sorts by severity (critical first) then documentCount. New convenience fields `criticalPatternCount` + `highPatternCount` for chip rendering. `AnalysesAggregation` + `DealAggregationDto` extended with `namedPatterns` array. Deal-detail API (`/api/deals/[id]/outcome`) extended to fetch `analyses[].toxicCombinations` (patternLabel + severity + toxicScore) and pass through. IcReadinessGate refactored to read `deal.aggregation.namedPatterns` / `criticalPatternCount` / `highPatternCount` directly — Gate 6 now covers ALL named patterns at critical severity (M&A + cross-domain), not just the 3 M&A-specific ones the prior client-side detection looked for. Backwards-compat: legacy ToxicCombination rows with null severity column → aggregator derives from toxicScore (80/60/40 thresholds); legacy AnalyzedDocument constructions without toxicCombinations field → namedPatterns: [], counts: 0 (no false-positive blockers). New vitest test file `src/lib/scoring/deal-aggregation.test.ts` locks the aggregation rules. **Forward-looking rule**: when adding new toxic-combination consumers (DealKanban chip, deal page header chip, analytics dashboard, future notifications), read from `aggregation.namedPatterns` — never re-implement the detection client-side. The "10-surface lockstep" cascade discipline now treats namedPatterns as the canonical signal.

**M&A cascade hard-layer ship (locked 2026-05-09 evening — Prisma + Pipeline + DQI proposals 1+2+3+4+5 from the proactive-surfacing audit).** Following the proactive-surfacing rule lock (see "When to Ask Questions" + Velocity & Scope Discipline §7), an architectural analysis surfaced 5 high-leverage hard-layer improvements that the prior cascade-depth audits had pre-shrunk away from. Founder green-lighted all 5 for full integration. Five commits ship across Prisma + scoring + pipeline + types: **(1) Document.parsedStructuredData JSON Prisma field + ToxicCombination.severity String** (commit `<this commit>`) — additive Prisma migration `20260509180000_mna_hard_layer_structured_data_severity` adds two columns: `Document.parsedStructuredData` carries type-aware structured parser output (today: synergy_model spreadsheets; future: qofe + integration_plan with their own `kind` discriminators) replacing the inline-marker text round-trip pattern in Document.content, and `ToxicCombination.severity` carries the canonical severity band ('critical'/'high'/'medium'/'low') derived from toxicScore at creation time so server-side queries can filter without re-deriving. New parser exports: `toParsedStructuredData(structure)` builds the JSON-persistable wrapper, `summariseSynergyDefensibility(parsed)` builds the DPR-cover summary directly from the persisted field. New file-parser export: `extractTypeAwareStructuredData(buffer, mimeType, filename, documentType)` runs in parallel to parseFile() at upload time. Upload route populates parsedStructuredData on Document.create with Prisma.InputJsonValue casting per the JSON-field convention; schema-drift fallback path gracefully degrades when column is missing. New `deriveSeverityFromScore(toxicScore)` utility + ToxicComboResult.severity field; persistToxicCombinations writes severity to the column with defensive fallback at the persistence boundary. Provenance-record assembler reads `Document.parsedStructuredData` first, falls back to inline-marker text extraction for legacy rows. Sparse index on (severity) WHERE severity IS NOT NULL so analytics queries scale.

**M&A cascade depth audit (locked 2026-05-09 evening — extends the cascade discipline beyond the 10-surface marketing cascade to engine + UI gates + DPR + taxonomy).** After the marketing/onboarding/parser ships landed, an audit found 12 surfaces that touch toxic combinations or document types that should have been updated alongside P1+P2. Of the 12, 9 were HIGH-leverage; 3 deepening commits closed them: (1) `cfdffdbc` engine — toxic-mitigation.ts gained 5-step PATTERN_PLAYBOOKS for Synergy Mirage / Conglomerate Fallacy / Winner's Curse anchored on BCG + McKinsey + KPMG + Kahneman & Lovallo + Porter + Zook research basis; reference-class-forecast.ts gained pattern-aware similarity boost (additive 0.15-0.30 capped, preserves existing scoring) so cases tagged with the same patternLabel as the audit's fired toxic combinations surface as analogs even when industries differ; cross-reference.ts gained 2 new conflict types (`synergy_assumption_mismatch`, `parenting_thesis_mismatch`) + M&A severity rule that forces Critical when synergy/parenting conflicts involve >25% of deal valuation; both insights/route.ts and provenance-record-data.ts updated to fetch `analysis.toxicCombinations` and pass `patternLabel`s into RCF. This keeps each commit cleanly scoped and the cascade cleanly diffable.

**(#1) compound-engine pattern-specific multipliers.** [src/lib/scoring/compound-engine.ts](src/lib/scoring/compound-engine.ts) gained pattern-specific bias-pair amplification anchored in research base rates: Synergy Mirage 1.75× (McKinsey/KPMG 70-90% miss rate), Winner's Curse 1.55× (Capen 1971, Bazerman & Samuelson 1983), Conglomerate Fallacy 1.65× (Lang & Stulz 1994 J Finance 50-65% diversification discount), The Yes Committee 1.55× (Microsoft-Nokia $249B), The Sunk Ship 1.55× (Lockheed Martin reach-forward losses). Implementation: new `PATTERN_PAIR_OVERRIDES` map + `getPatternOverrideWeight()` helper. `getInteractionWeight()` priority chain extended to check pattern overrides between caller-supplied weights (priority 1) and the ontology matrix (priority 3). New `firedPatternLabels: string[]` option on `computeCompoundScore` — threaded through `computeBiasCompoundSeverity → getInteractionWeight`. New "named_pattern_amplification" adjustment line surfaces fired patterns by name in `CompoundScore.adjustments`. **Backwards-compat**: every existing caller omits `firedPatternLabels` → engine runs the legacy 4-step priority chain unchanged. Platform-baseline Brier 0.258 unchanged (seed library cases don't pass firedPatternLabels through `computeSyntheticDQI`; SYNTHETIC_WEIGHTS_LEGACY_2_0_0 pin already protects the DQI weight side from drift). **Pipeline ACTIVATED 2026-05-09 evening (M&A cascade follow-through ship):** [src/lib/learning/named-patterns.ts](src/lib/learning/named-patterns.ts) gained a pure-function `matchNamedPatterns({ biasTypes, context })` matcher mirroring the persisted detector's biasTypes-subset + matchesContext semantics but without the Prisma round-trip. Wired into [src/lib/agents/nodes.ts](src/lib/agents/nodes.ts) `riskScorerNode` BEFORE the two `computeCompoundScore` calls (calibrated + baseline tracks). Both compound-score paths now pass `firedPatternLabels` so PATTERN_PAIR_OVERRIDES amplifications fire on every live audit. Conservative posture: context fields the in-flight matcher cannot derive from pipeline state (timePressure / unanimousConsensus) stay undefined → patterns requiring them won't false-fire (the persisted toxic-combinations.ts detector with full Prisma context catches them post-audit instead). 15-test regression suite at [src/lib/learning/named-patterns.test.ts](src/lib/learning/named-patterns.test.ts) locks the matcher's behaviour: case-insensitive bias-type matching, monetaryStakes ladder upgrade ('high' required → 'very_high' matches), partial-context matching, multi-pattern detection. **Activation discipline**: the persisted detector still runs after audit completion for analytics + ToxicCombination persistence. The pipeline matcher is the in-flight signal-extraction path used for compound-engine amplification AND DQI 7th-component compoundRisk scoring. Both paths are armed.

**Forward-looking rule for the cascade discipline**: every named-pattern surface reads from the canonical NAMED_PATTERNS export. New consumers (analytics dashboards, deal-page chips, future internal tooling) MUST import NAMED_PATTERNS rather than re-implementing the catalogue. Same lockstep discipline as the bias-taxonomy cascade.

**Synergy model parser deepening (locked 2026-05-09):** new `src/lib/parsers/` directory with two modules — `synergy-defensibility.ts` (pure-function scorer over a single synergy claim with `hasMechanism / hasOwner / hasMilestone` flags + claim-type → BCG/McKinsey base-rate band: revenue 30-50%, cost_cogs 60-80%, cost_opex 50-70%, capex 60-80%, unknown 30-80%; returns severity `critical/high/medium/low` + `aggregateDefensibility` portfolio summary) and `synergy-model-parser.ts` (consumes an ExcelJS workbook, detects synergy-shaped sheets via name keywords or first-8-rows context match, finds the header row by ≥2 amount-shaped column headers, extracts each row with a label + numeric amounts as a `SynergyClaim`, classifies the claim type from row label + sheet name, scores defensibility via the scorer, returns a `SynergyStructure` with sheets / claims / total Y1 / total run-rate / portfolio defensibility / confidence band; pure function over the workbook, no I/O). `parseFile()` in `src/lib/utils/file-parser.ts` extended with optional `documentType` parameter — when an `.xlsx` is uploaded as `synergy_model`, the parser runs `extractSynergyStructure` and prepends the procurement-grade `STRUCTURED SYNERGY MODEL — PARSED PRE-AUDIT` block to the flattened sheet text so the structurer + biasDetective see per-claim defensibility data without a new state field on the audit graph (per the "Modifying the analysis pipeline" rule — graph.ts unchanged). The `synergy_model` overlay prompt in `src/lib/prompts/investment-vertical.ts` extended to instruct the bias detective to USE the structured block as primary evidence (not re-derive from flattened text) and apply explicit critical-severity flagging rules (any claim at critical → portfolio-level Critical; portfolio fullyDefendedPct < 50% → High; revenue-share > 50% with fullyDefendedPct < 70% → High citing the realisation gap). **Critical bug fix shipped same commit:** `/api/upload/route.ts` `VALID_DOC_TYPES` was hardcoded to 6 entries while `INVESTMENT_DOCUMENT_TYPES` had grown to 9 — silently rejecting `synergy_model` / `qofe` / `integration_plan` uploads since the 2026-05-09 P1 ship. Migrated to `[...INVESTMENT_DOCUMENT_TYPES, 'other']` so future additions to the canonical export propagate automatically. **Forward-looking rule**: when adding new M&A document subtypes that should support type-aware parser enrichment, follow the same pattern — new `src/lib/parsers/<subtype>-parser.ts` module + extend `parseFile()` with a conditional branch keyed on documentType + extend the DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS prompt to reference the inline-marker block. Don't add new audit-graph state fields; embed structured data inline in text content under canonical markers so downstream nodes consume it without graph modification.

**M&A onboarding deepening (extended 2026-05-09 — second onboarding pass after the data + visibility ships):** the first onboarding pass updated the four `ma` surfaces with the new patterns + document types. This pass adds depth at the welcome moment + tour + first-run + dashboard subtitle so an M&A user sees buyer-fit signal at every entry point. Five surfaces touched: (i) `src/components/ui/WelcomeModal.tsx` — new `VALUE_PROPS_BY_ROLE` map with role-specific value-prop cards (eyebrow + headline + 3 bullets per role) rendered between role-pick and CTAs. The `ma` card names Synergy Mirage detector + Conglomerate Fallacy + Winner's Curse + IC Readiness Gate's 5 gates. Type-system enforces `Record<Role, ...>` so adding a new role requires adding its value-prop in the same commit. (ii) `src/components/onboarding/OnboardingTour.tsx` — `TOUR_STEPS_BY_ROLE.ma` expanded from 3 → 4 stops. New `SHARED_STOP_DEALS` selector + a Projects/Deals stop inserted between Upload and Usage that lands the deal-as-atomic-decision-unit framing + IC Readiness Gate's 5 gates. The 4th cross-doc stop sharpened to mention IRR/MOIC calibration on the Outcome Flywheel. (iii) `src/components/ui/Sidebar.tsx` — added `id="onborda-nav-deals"` to the Projects NavItem (mirrors the existing `id="onborda-nav-analytics"` pattern; the only sidebar IDs of this shape are tour anchors, so adding new tour stops requires this same single-line change). (iv) `src/components/onboarding/FirstRunInlineWalkthrough.tsx` `ROLE_PITCH.ma` rewritten to reflect the now-six M&A specimens (3 original + Project Marlin / Helix / Apex) and name the three toxic combinations they fire. (v) `src/app/(platform)/dashboard/page.tsx` `ROLE_DASHBOARD_SUBTITLE.ma` rewritten to name the three toxic combinations directly — first thing an M&A user sees on every dashboard load is the named-pattern vocabulary. **Forward-looking rule**: when a new role lands in the Role enum, add a `VALUE_PROPS_BY_ROLE` entry + `ROLE_DASHBOARD_SUBTITLE` entry + `ROLE_PITCH` entry + `TOUR_STEPS_BY_ROLE` entry + `Onborda steps` registration in the same commit. The TypeScript `Record<Role, ...>` shapes enforce most of this at compile time, but the Onborda registration is by-runtime so easy to miss — see "Onborda Tour Registration Discipline" lock above.

**M&A onboarding surfaces (locked 2026-05-09 alongside the P1 ship):** the `ma` role across the four onboarding surfaces names the new patterns + document types directly so a Head of Corp Dev / PE Deal Partner sees the M&A-workflow-native depth the moment they sign up. (i) `src/lib/data/sample-bundles.ts` — three new real-anchor specimens authored to fire ONE toxic combo each: `MA_PROJECT_MARLIN` (Synergy Mirage / AOL-Time Warner content-distribution shape), `MA_PROJECT_HELIX` (Conglomerate Fallacy / Daimler-Chrysler diversified-platform shape), `MA_PROJECT_APEX` (Winner's Curse / WeWork S-1 competitive-process shape). The `bundlesForRole(null|'other')` no-role branch refactored from literal indices to filter-based (find first per role) so adding new bundles can never silently break the breadth view. (ii) `src/components/onboarding/OnboardingTour.tsx` `TOUR_STEPS_BY_ROLE.ma` — three stops sharpened to name 9 supported document types (IC memo, CIM, QofE, synergy model, integration plan, term sheet, model, due diligence, counsel review) + Synergy Mirage / Conglomerate Fallacy / Winner's Curse by name in the upload stop, IC Readiness Gate (5 gates) named in the cross-doc stop.
