The cold-start moment is where buyer-fit signal lands.

**QofE parser ship (locked 2026-05-09, M&A hard-layer extension — second parser pattern):** new [src/lib/parsers/qofe-defensibility.ts](src/lib/parsers/qofe-defensibility.ts) (deterministic phrase-pattern scorer with 6 canonical red-flag rules — recurring "one-time" / owner-comp full add-back / speculative run-rate / cherry-picked WC peg / customer-concentration undisclosed / sell-side commission signal — anchored in BCG diligence frameworks + Bain "Adjusted EBITDA Reality Check") + [src/lib/parsers/qofe-parser.ts](src/lib/parsers/qofe-parser.ts) (`extractQofeStructure(text)` returns `ParsedQofeData` wrapper, `formatQofeAssessmentForAudit(parsed)` emits a "STRUCTURED QOFE — PARSED PRE-AUDIT" inline-marker block mirroring the synergy_model pattern). [src/lib/utils/file-parser.ts](src/lib/utils/file-parser.ts) extended with TWO branches: (a) `parseFile()` PDF branch — when `documentType === 'qofe'` and the upload is a .pdf, runs the QofE scorer over the extracted text and prepends the structured block above the flattened narrative; (b) `extractTypeAwareStructuredData()` — returns `ParsedQofeData` for persistence to `Document.parsedStructuredData` JSONB column (same generic column the synergy_model parser uses, discriminated by `kind: 'qofe' | 'synergy_model'`). The `qofe` `DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS` prompt in `investment-vertical.ts` extended to instruct the bias detective to USE the structured block as primary evidence (not re-derive from flattened text) and apply explicit critical-severity flagging rules (any structured-block flag at critical → fire Synergy Mirage / Sunk Ship at Critical with verbatim verdict; sell-side commissioned + 2+ flags → fire Synergy Mirage at High citing Seller-Halo Filter; customer-concentration undisclosed → fire authority_bias / disposition_effect at Medium). 17-test scorer regression suite at [src/lib/parsers/qofe-defensibility.test.ts](src/lib/parsers/qofe-defensibility.test.ts) — locks all 6 red-flag detection rules + commission-signal extraction + EBITDA-density signal + portfolio-severity max + matched-phrase capture for transparency. **Inverted rule design** (customer-concentration undisclosed): only fires when the text actually looks like a QofE — gated on (a) ≥3 distinct QofE-vocabulary hits AND (b) inflation signal ≥0.05 OR (c) 2+ other QofE flags already fired. Prevents false-positives on non-QofE memos that incidentally mention "Quality of Earnings" once. **Forward-looking rule** (mirrors the synergy parser pattern): when adding new M&A document subtypes that need type-aware parser enrichment, follow the same 4-shape lockstep: (1) new `src/lib/parsers/<subtype>-defensibility.ts` pure scorer + tests; (2) new `src/lib/parsers/<subtype>-parser.ts` with `extractXStructure(input)` + `formatXForAudit(parsed)` + persistable `kind: '<subtype>'` wrapper; (3) `extractTypeAwareStructuredData()` branch + `parseFile()` enrichment branch; (4) `DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS.<subtype>` updated to reference the inline-marker block as primary evidence.

**The build roadmap** (originally written 2026-05-09 against a pre-AI-pair-programming quarterly cadence; actual velocity recalibrated 2026-05-09 evening — see "Velocity & Scope Discipline" section below):

- **P1 — IC Memo / CIM parser type-recognition + 5 first-class M&A toxic combinations.** SHIPPED 2026-05-09 (commit `cfdffdbc`).
- **P2 — Synergy Validation Overlay + Boardroom Decision Twin REFINEMENT.** Synergy Validation Overlay SHIPPED 2026-05-09 evening (commit `9eddb2c`) as a structured ExcelJS parser + per-claim defensibility scorer + base-rate realisation bands per BCG/McKinsey. Boardroom Decision Twin refinement (sharpening for IC vote-prediction specifically) deferred — not blocking and the existing simulator already runs the boardroom flow.
- **P2.5 — Pipeline activation of `firedPatternLabels` + qofe parser ship.** Both SHIPPED 2026-05-09 evening: matchNamedPatterns wired into riskScorerNode (compound-engine PATTERN_PAIR_OVERRIDES amplifications now fire on every live audit) + qofe parser deterministic scorer + 6-rule red-flag detector + parsedStructuredData persistence. The first non-synergy parser landing on the canonical generic JSONB column.
- **P3 — Deal-stage UI overlays (Sourcing → Diligence → IC Review → Closing visible in the product chrome).** Pure demo polish for acqui-hire conversations. Estimated 1-2 sessions to ship the full cascade.
- **Backlog (post-acqui-hire) — PMI / integration_plan parser + UI overlays.** Feedback loop is 12-24 months, too slow for solo founder. Wait until inside the acquirer with an engineering team. (The integration_plan document subtype + DOC_TYPE_OVERLAYS overlay text already exists; the structured parser is what's deferred.)

**Forward-looking rule**: when adding M&A-specific overlays, prefer ENHANCING existing biases / patterns / document types over creating new ones. The 22-bias taxonomy is the structural moat; M&A specificity comes from compound-pattern detection + document-type overlay prompts, not from 30+ M&A-specific biases that would dilute the taxonomy. The named M&A patterns earn their first-class status by appearing in the 143-case library at materially higher frequency than non-M&A patterns.

## Positioning & Vocabulary (locked 2026-04-13)

**Core value proposition:** "The Four Moments We Catch What Others Miss" — a Decision Knowledge Graph as the foundation, with (1) the Graph itself, (2) predicting CEO/steering-committee questions, (3) auditing reasoning, and (4) closing the outcome loop via DQI.

**LinkedIn content → landing page bridge:** Bias case studies on famous corporate decisions (Kodak, Blockbuster, Nokia, etc.) warm up the traffic. The landing page says: "The same lens that exposed [X] now audits your strategic memos in 60 seconds."

**Native vocabulary to use:**

- "strategic memo" (primary artifact — the analog to "investment memo")
- "board deck" (the artifact that gets presented)
- "strategic recommendation" / "market-entry recommendation"
- "steering committee" / "executive review" / "board"
- "CEO, board, or parent company" (the stakeholders)
- "Decision Knowledge Graph" (always full name)
- "Decision Quality Index" / "DQI"
- "quarter after quarter" (cadence)
- "143 historical decisions" (benchmark number — derived from `HISTORICAL_CASE_COUNT = ALL_CASES.length` in [src/lib/data/case-studies/index.ts](src/lib/data/case-studies/index.ts); was 135 in the 2026-04-16 dedup, grew to 143 with the emerging-markets failure cases + new success cases through 2026-04-29; production copy MUST import the constant rather than hardcoding the number)
- "22-bias R²F taxonomy" / "DI-B-001 → DI-B-022" — the canonical taxonomy phrasing. Derive the count from `Object.keys(BIAS_EDUCATION).length` per the canonical-import discipline (see Bias Taxonomy cascade rule #11). The legacy "30+ cognitive biases" phrasing is **deprecated 2026-05-13** (CR-3 audit fix): the taxonomy is 22 IDs (DI-B-001 → DI-B-022); the "+" was a hedge against a stale count and conflicts with the precise audit-trail discipline procurement readers expect
- **"native system of record for strategic reasoning"** — the category-defining phrase (2026-04-22 lock). Lives in the landing H1, /how-it-works subtitle, pitch deck slide 2. Softer alternative "native medium for strategic reasoning" is interchangeable for surfaces where "system of record" feels over-procurement-coded.
- **"Recognition-Rigor Framework" / "R²F"** — the category-defining framework name (2026-04-22 lock). Kahneman's rigor (System 2 debiasing) + Klein's recognition (System 1 amplification) arbitrated in one pipeline. Trademark filing DEFERRED until pre-seed close; use consistently now so vocabulary is owned by usage alone. Anchor citation: 2009 Kahneman-Klein paper "Conditions for Intuitive Expertise: a failure to disagree." **R²F is operationalised through specific paper-application surfaces, not just naming**: (a) BIAS_DETECTIVE_PROMPT in `src/lib/agents/prompts.ts` runs validity-aware scoring — confidence-language is penalised harder in low-validity domains (M&A, market entry, long-horizon strategy) than in high-validity ones (per the 2009 paper's first condition for trustworthy intuition); (b) DI-B-021 (`illusion_of_validity`) is the first-class detector for the 2009 paper's central finding — narrative coherence creating false confidence — wired through the bias taxonomy + compound interactions ("Coherent Confidence" toxic combo: Illusion of Validity + Overconfidence + Confirmation/Halo); (c) pre-mortem prompts (3 surfaces in `prompts.ts`) enforce Klein & Mitchell 1995 / Mitchell-Russo-Pennington 1989 prospective-hindsight framing in past tense — "the failure began when…", "the warning sign everyone missed was…" — which produces 25-30% more failure-cause insights than conditional voice; (d) `src/lib/learning/feedback-adequacy.ts` audits the 2009 paper's SECOND condition for trustworthy intuition (adequate opportunity to learn from rapid feedback) by scoring the user's closed-outcome history per domain and surfacing a verdict band (adequate / sparse / cold_start / unknown) on every DPR cover page. **All four operationalisations were locked 2026-04-30 in the paper-application sprint.** When extending R²F further, reach for the ranking of remaining 7 paper applications captured in the same sprint commit message before adding new surfaces.
- **"decision archaeology"** — the canonical verb for the pain we replace (reconstructing past reasoning from the 4-tool graveyard).
- **"four-tool graveyard"** — Google Docs drafts / Slack threads / Confluence writeups / the board deck. Canonical pain name, used in the What-we-replace beat.

**Vocabulary discipline by reader temperature (locked 2026-04-26 — resolves the contradiction surfaced by NotebookLM strategic synthesis between the global vocabulary lock and the cold-context bd_8 lesson):**

The locked vocabulary above ("native reasoning layer," "R²F," "DQI," "DPR — hashed + tamper-evident") is the WARM-CONTEXT default. Cold contexts require a descriptive bridge that doesn't borrow pre-existing academic vocabulary.

- **Warm contexts** (second meeting onward, pitch decks, pricing pages, design-partner conversations, internal Founder Hub, anything where the reader has already signalled interest): use the locked category vocabulary. "Native reasoning layer for every high-stakes call." "Recognition-Rigor Framework arbitrating Kahneman + Klein." "Decision Quality Index in 60 seconds." This is the ownable claim and where category creation happens.
- **Cold contexts** (LinkedIn DM opener, cold email subject + first line, conference 1:1 introduction, landing-page above-the-fold for unaware traffic): use descriptive plain-language phrases. "60-second audit on a strategic memo." "Pre-IC audit layer." "Strategic memo audits." "Decision quality auditing." NEVER use Kahneman's "decision hygiene" (his 2021 _Noise_ term — borrowing it cedes our category vocabulary to a more famous author). NEVER lead cold with "reasoning layer" — the reader hasn't earned the term yet and will scroll past.
- **The bridge sentence** (the move that converts cold → warm in two beats): "We run 60-second audits on strategic memos. The technical name is a reasoning layer — Recognition-Rigor Framework, scored as a Decision Quality Index." Practise this transition until it lands in 10 seconds. Every cold-context surface should set up this upgrade.

**Vocabulary to AVOID:**

- "thesis" (PE/VC-coded)
- "investment memo" / "IC" / "investment committee" (PE-coded)
- "LP" / "fund" (PE-coded)
- "deal" as a headline term (too M&A-narrow; use "call" or "memo")
- "M&A documents" as primary artifact (use "strategic memo" first; M&A is secondary)
- "12-node pipeline" in headline positions (too technical for CSO buyer; fine as technical detail only)
- **"decision intelligence platform"** in marketing leads — Gartner-crowded (Peak.ai, Cloverpop, Quantellia, Aera). Use "native system of record for strategic reasoning" instead. "Decision intelligence" is fine as a descriptor inside a sentence; never as the headline claim.
- "human-AI governance system" as an H1 (retired 2026-04-22 in favor of system-of-record framing).

**Tone:** Calm CSO 1:1 voice with manager-level pain included. Never critique the buyer's judgment. Frame as additive rigor, not a report card. Lead with gain, not deficit. Use em dashes sparingly (one or two for emphasis); prefer commas and sentence breaks.

## Regulatory Tailwinds (locked 2026-04-22)

**The positioning claim:** Decision Intel is built for the regulatory wave already in motion. The Decision Provenance Record is "the record your AI-augmented decision-making is already supposed to produce" — proactive, not reactive.

**Named tailwinds to reference (by date + status, in every investor conversation):**

- **EU AI Act** — in force since Aug 2024. Prohibited practices enforceable Feb 2, 2025. General-purpose AI obligations Aug 2, 2025. High-risk decision-support systems Aug 2, 2026. Articles 13 (transparency), 14 (human oversight), 15 (accuracy + record-keeping), Annex III (high-risk use cases). **This is the anchor tailwind — the DPR maps onto Art 14 record-keeping by design.**
- **SEC AI Disclosure** — proposed rulemaking 2024, evolving through 2026 for AI use in investment-adviser decisions. DPR's model lineage + prompt fingerprint + judge variance are the documentation.
- **Basel III · Pillar 2 ICAAP** — live for regulated banks. Requires documented internal-capital-adequacy process including qualitative decisions. DPR attaches a Basel III provision to every flagged bias.
- **UK AI White Paper** — pro-innovation, principles-based (Mar 2023). Regulator guidance across FCA, ICO, and CMA converges on transparency, fairness, accountability, contestability. The DPR is the contestable artifact by default.
- **SOX §404** — live for public companies. Internal-controls documentation.
- **SEC Reg D** — live for private placements. Forward-looking-statement disclosure rigor.
- **GDPR Art. 22** — live since 2018. Automated-decision rights require meaningful information about the logic involved; DPR citations provide that without exposing platform IP.
- **Colorado SB24-205** (AI anti-discrimination, Feb 2026 enforceable) and **California SB942** (AI transparency disclosures) — secondary US tailwinds; reference when selling into CO/CA-based public companies.
- **AI Verify Foundation** (Singapore IMDA, Apache 2.0, aligned with EU + OECD) — 11 internationally-recognised AI governance principles: transparency, explainability, repeatability, safety, security, robustness, fairness, data governance, accountability, human agency & oversight, inclusive growth. Every DPR field maps onto these principles. Canonical mapping page at `/regulatory/ai-verify`. **Language discipline is critical here: AI Verify is self-assessment, not third-party certification. The accurate and defensible claim is "aligned with the 11 internationally-recognised AI governance principles codified by AI Verify" — NEVER "fully compliant" or "certified by." The AI Verify Foundation's own FAQ states the framework "does not guarantee that any AI system tested will be free from risks or biases or is completely safe"; we mirror that disclaimer on the mapping page.** Ship-what-we-have moves: the mapping page. Deferred to the Regulatory Tailwind moat-stack work: contributing a plugin to AI Verify 2.0's stock-plugins directory (would land DI in an IMDA-adjacent open framework's official codebase — highest-leverage free regulatory credential once engineering bandwidth exists).

**The framing rule:** when writing about regulation, lead with what's already in force or calendared, not with what might pass someday. Enterprise procurement believes calendars and skeptical of "the FTC is thinking about…" framing. Every tailwind we reference has either a statute, a regulator guidance, or an enforcement date. If it doesn't, don't cite it.

**Where this lives on marketing surfaces:**

- `/security` — dedicated "Regulatory tailwinds · already in motion" section with 6 tailwinds cards, each with status + date + how the DPR covers it.
- `/design-partner` — compact "Why now" strip above the fold.
- `/pricing` — trust band includes "Decision Provenance Record: signed + hashed on every audit."
- `/how-it-works` — pipeline-node academic-anchor column already cites regulatory provisions; keep it aligned.
- Pitch deck — slide 3 (Why Now) pairs the three anchor tailwinds (EU AI Act Aug 2026, SEC 2024-2026, Basel III live) with the DPR as the answer.

**Where this DOES NOT live:**

- The landing page — deliberately kept clean. Regulation is a secondary beat for CSOs; they arrive via the R²F story first, then discover tailwinds on `/security` once procurement surfaces.
- Demo / free-tier surfaces — tailwinds conversation belongs in the procurement-stage conversation, not the discovery-stage one.

## Marketing Voice — Enterprise Discipline (locked 2026-04-19)

**The single test:** every word on a marketing surface must be something a Fortune 500 CSO, GC, or CFO could say aloud in a procurement meeting without flinching. If it reads like a startup talking to itself, cut it.

**Marketing surfaces this rule governs:** `/`, `/demo`, `/how-it-works`, `/case-studies`, `/proof`, `/bias-genome`, `/security`, `/privacy`, `/pricing`, any landing-page module, any email or LinkedIn copy.

**Banned on marketing surfaces — no exceptions:**

- Stage-of-company language: "pre-seed", "seed-stage", "pre-revenue", "we just launched", "we're building", "we're a young company", "solo founder", "early days", "our journey", "just shipped"
- Apologetic proof framing: "we don't have logos yet", "we're still cold-starting", "pilots coming soon", "waiting for our first customer"
- Technical jargon: "12-node pipeline", "LangGraph", "agent", "agents", "3 independent AI judges", "pgvector", "prompts", "tokens", "inference", model names, any infra term
- Startup-cute visual patterns: "Sparkles" icons on category pills, "The category we're defining" framed as a self-congratulatory badge, rounded-pill "look at us" banners, marketing-page glitter
- Loss-first headlines: "X% of strategy fails", "Most decisions are wrong", "Stop getting it wrong" — lead with gain, not deficit
- Vague jargon: "game-changer", "revolutionary", "next-generation", "AI-powered" (on its own), "leveraging AI"
- **Named unsigned prospects, design-partner names, or any "`{firm}`-class buyers" coding** in production HTML, JSON-LD, or metadata. Confidentiality of every active conversation is procurement-grade. The 2026-04-25 audit caught `Sankore-class buyers` rendered on `/security`; the discipline is permanent. When you need to signal a regional / persona expansion in copy, use the abstract regional or persona-class noun ("African markets," "Fortune 500 strategy team," "EM funds") — never the specific firm or person.
- **Inconsistent count copy.** When the same artefact, framework set, or feature count appears in more than one place, derive it from the source-of-truth array (e.g. `${FRAMEWORKS.length}` or `getAllRegisteredFrameworks().length` from [@/lib/compliance/frameworks](src/lib/compliance/frameworks/index.ts)) so it cannot drift. The 2026-04-25 audit caught `/security` shipping "17 frameworks" in the hero subhead and "Seven frameworks, mapped flag-by-flag" in a section heading on the same page — exactly the inconsistency a procurement reader circles in red. The 2026-04-27 audit caught `StartHereTab.tsx:418` hardcoding "17 frameworks" on the Founder Hub Current Positioning Anchor card; same class, different surface. Fixed to `getAllRegisteredFrameworks().length`. The fix is structural (derived count), not editorial. **Forward-looking rule**: any new copy that mentions a framework count, bias count, audit count, or pipeline-node count must derive from the canonical source array in the same line — never literal a number that could drift when the array changes.

**Allowed and encouraged:**

- Capability-led leads: "Causal reasoning, not correlation dressed up as insight" — name the capability, not the problem
- Concrete artefacts: "strategic memo", "board deck", "audit committee", "steering committee", "Decision Provenance Record" (2026-04-22 rename from "Audit Defense Packet"), "Decision Knowledge Graph", "Decision Quality Index"
- Compliance vocabulary: SOC 2, GDPR, EU AI Act, Basel III, SEC Reg D — specific, named, defensible
- Enterprise shapes: the audit committee, the GC review, the procurement bar, the regulator meeting
- Numbers that survive due diligence: "143 audited corporate decisions" (derive from `HISTORICAL_CASE_COUNT`), "30+ cognitive biases", "~90% blended margin" — publicly verifiable or internally defensible
- Quiet confidence: "checkable", "traceable", "defensible", "one click away, no login, no gate"

**Where the jargon CAN live:** `/how-it-works` is the only public page that can name the 12-node pipeline, the node zones, and the interaction matrix — and even there, the manifest in `src/lib/data/pipeline-nodes.ts` is the ceiling. Founder Hub, Founder School, and the pitch deck can be as technical as useful because they're behind Supabase auth or the founder's own outreach.

**PSV vs artifact-led — applies by surface type (locked 2026-04-26 — resolves the contradiction surfaced by NotebookLM strategic synthesis between the marketing-leads-with-PSV memory and the new specimen-audit lessons es_10 + gtm_8):**

The Problem→Solution→Value memory rule and the "specimen DPR IS the pitch" lessons are not in conflict; they apply to different surfaces. The principle: **PSV when the reader has zero context about you; artifact-led when you can target a specific reader with a specific artefact they'll recognise.**

- **Broadcast / unaware-traffic surfaces** (landing-page above-the-fold, public marketing pages, top-of-funnel ads, generic conference talks): apply PSV strictly. Lead with the buyer's pain at scale (McKinsey 8% / strategy beyond hockey stick, $250M/yr per F500), then the solution shape (R²F audit pipeline), then the value delivered (board-ready artefact). NEVER lead with the product artefact (DPR / DQI / R²F as first impressions per the empathic-mode-first rule). The reader has not yet earned the product vocabulary.
- **Direct outbound surfaces** (cold email to a named prospect, LinkedIn DM with a specific person in mind, design-partner discovery call, named conference 1:1): the specimen artefact (WeWork or Dangote DPR PDF, attached or linked) IS the pitch. Cold emails with the DPR attached convert higher than 3-paragraph PSV emails because the artefact does the persuasion in a way 3 paragraphs cannot. Treat the DPR as the empathic-mode move — the buyer recognises the document, sees the audit, draws their own conclusion before you ask anything.
- **The geographic specimen choice (per gtm_8):** US/global prospect → WeWork S-1; African / EM-focused fund → Dangote 2014 Pan-African expansion; cross-border buyer → both, in sequence.

Both PSV and artifact-led are honest moves — the surface determines which fits. Don't apply PSV to a targeted DM with the WeWork audit attached (you'll under-leverage the artefact). Don't lead the public landing page with "here's our DPR" (you'll burn the cold reader before they understand the problem).

**If Claude drifts into startup voice:** stop, reread this section, rewrite. A correction from the founder on voice is a tripwire — update this section in the same commit so the next session has the lesson baked in.

## External Attack Vectors (locked 2026-04-26 — surfaced by NotebookLM external pre-mortem, saved as note `9a249bd8` in master KB `809f5104`)

The internal-execution pre-mortems (cathedral-of-code, outcome-gate avoidance, infinite-pilot trap) are addressed by the outcome-gate enforcement + the design-partner contractual asks codified in `es_11`. The OUTSIDE-IN attack vectors are different — what could a competitor / regulator / market context do that derails Decision Intel regardless of execution quality? Three identified, each load-bearing:

**1. Cloverpop's data advantage.** Cloverpop was acquired in September 2025 by Clearbox Decisions specifically to commercialize for enterprise. They market "Generative AI" + "Synthesis AI" capabilities. **The fatal threat:** our defensible moat is the per-org Brier-scored outcome-recalibration flywheel; Cloverpop has years of structured enterprise decision + outcome data we don't have yet. If Clearbox simply licenses GPT-4o or Claude to run a Kahneman-style bias prompt over their massive existing repository of logged decisions, they instantly replicate "audit" capability backed by REAL historical data. We have the prompts; they have the data. **Defensive moves:** (a) Outcome Gate Enforcement (Phase 1 shipped 2026-04-26) accelerates outcome-data accumulation for design-partner orgs — every gated audit forces the loop closure that builds OUR data moat. (b) Pan-African specimen library (WeWork + Dangote + future co-authored sectoral specimens) compounds in dimensions Cloverpop can't easily extend (regional regulatory + sovereign-context expertise + cross-border deal patterns). (c) The 17-framework regulatory map across G7 / EU / GCC / African markets is structurally something a US-incumbent would need 12-18 months to match.

**2. IBM watsonx.governance bundling.** IBM launched massive Q1 2026 updates to watsonx.governance explicitly targeting EU AI Risk Assessments + automated compliance accelerators. **The fatal threat:** we argue we audit the _human decision_ and IBM audits the _model_ — but Fortune 500 General Counsels do not want to buy two separate governance SKUs. If IBM adds a basic "Human Decision Provenance" module to their existing entrenched watsonx suite, F500 CSOs and GCs will check the EU AI Act Article 14 compliance box with IBM by August 2026 enforcement deadline. A 16-year-old's standalone $30K/year platform cannot beat IBM bundling motion when the GC is rushing to meet enforcement. **Defensive moves:** (a) Pan-African / EM-fund wedge is the bypass — IBM doesn't sell into Pan-African corp dev or EM-focused fund partners with the depth + cultural rooting we have. Win the wedge before IBM bundles. (b) The DPR's Pan-African regulatory mapping (NDPR / CBN / WAEMU / PoPIA / CMA Kenya) is something IBM watsonx does NOT cover — that's the procurement-cycle accelerator no IBM bundle replaces. (c) Long-term: position Decision Intel as the audit layer that integrates WITH IBM watsonx rather than competes — but only after the wedge is established + the references exist.

**3. The agentic shift makes the strategic memo obsolete.** Palantir launched its "Agentic AI Hives" manifesto. Databricks is positioning Unity Catalog as an agent control tower. Aera Technology is deploying autonomous agents that execute supply-chain decisions directly. Snowflake is pitching agents acting over governed data. **Citation-grade evidence (sourced 2026-05-02):** WEF Future of Jobs 2030 projects 92M global jobs eliminated by 2030 across information-intensive sectors + 170M new roles requiring hyper-specialized human-AI collaboration; the British Standards Institution seven-economy study finds 31% of organizations evaluate AI before considering hiring + 41% of leaders confirm AI is actively reducing headcount + 25% believe most entry-level cognitive tasks can be done by AI today; the Agentic Task Exposure (ATE) framework projects 93.2% of analyzed occupations across information-intensive sectors (finance, law, healthcare support, sales, administration) cross moderate-to-high displacement risk over 2025-2030; LeCun / Meta AMI's Joint Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) pushes toward causal World Models with mass commercialization forecast 2026-2030. **The fatal threat:** our entire product is built around uploading a written "strategic memo" — but the volume of human-authored 40-page strategy memos may plummet as enterprises shift from decision-SUPPORT to decision-EXECUTION via agents. We're building the ultimate spell-checker for a document format the enterprise is actively trying to automate away.

**Defensive moves — the existing product is more structurally protective than the threat framing suggests** (locked 2026-05-02 with the agentic-shift investigation scaffolding, see [docs/agentic-shift-investigation-q2-2026.md](docs/agentic-shift-investigation-q2-2026.md)): (a) **Authorship-agnostic R²F.** The 22-bias DI-B-001 → DI-B-022 taxonomy fires on REASONING PATTERNS inside artefacts, not on artefact format. DI-B-021 (illusion_of_validity) detects narrative coherence not backed by base rates — this pattern appears in agent outputs the SAME way it appears in human memos, arguably more cleanly because LLM auto-regression prioritizes coherence by construction. DI-B-022 (inside_view_dominance) detects projections without grounded comparables — agent-authored memos lacking explicit reference-class anchors trigger this detector at HIGHER rates than human memos. As agent-authored strategic artefacts proliferate, R²F detection becomes MORE valuable, not less. The moat compounds, it doesn't erode. (b) **DPR is the contractual artefact regardless of input source.** EU AI Act Article 14 + Basel III Pillar 2 ICAAP + SEC AI disclosure rules require auditable records for HIGH-STAKES decisions, not for human-authored decisions specifically. The DPR's hashed + tamper-evident provenance with six R²F cover signals + 19-framework regulatory mapping is the contractual answer the F500 GC needs whether the input was a 40-page memo or an agent decision-chain log. The artefact lock is on what gets PRESERVED, not what gets AUDITED. (c) **The pipeline accepts structured artefacts, not just memos.** The structurer node already normalizes input shape before downstream nodes fire. Extending the input schema from "uploaded document" to "agent decision-chain log" or "agent system prompt + output trace" is an INPUT-LAYER change, not a pipeline rewrite — the 12-node pipeline + 20×20 toxic-combinations matrix + 143-case reference-class engine work the same way once the input is structured. (d) **The 7-minute live audit motion on specimens (es_10) doesn't depend on memo format.** (e) **Pan-African / EM-fund wedge bypass** — IBM watsonx + Palantir + Snowflake don't sell into Pan-African corp dev or EM-focused funds with the depth + cultural rooting we have; agentic-platform competitors are weakest where DI is strongest.

**The investigation lock-step (per GTM v3.3 §5):** 30-day parallel investigation in May-June 2026, sample 10 prospects via warm intros (Mr. Reiner + Mr. Gabe networks) with the discovery question _"How are your strategic acquisition memos and IC decks being authored today — fully human, AI-assisted, or agent-generated?"_ Three forward paths captured in [docs/agentic-shift-investigation-q2-2026.md](docs/agentic-shift-investigation-q2-2026.md): Path A (human-authored dominant >70%) → wedge holds, audit-layer-for-agents stays Q1 2027 reserve; Path B (AI-assisted 40-70%) → wedge holds + ship AI-assistance signature detector as next R²F paper application; Path C (agent-generated >30%) → extend structurer input schema for agent decision-chain logs in 2026 H2, position DI as audit layer for STRATEGIC DECISIONS regardless of input format. End-of-June 2026 deliverable: one-page synthesis memo with the path locked on evidence. The founder finds out NOW, not in October.

**The unplanned blind spot synthesis (2026-04-26 NotebookLM external pre-mortem):** _"You are wedged into a shrinking middle ground. You are fighting over the human-written memo just as Palantir and Databricks eliminate it via agentic execution, and you are trying to sell a standalone compliance artefact just as IBM bundles that exact compliance into their monolithic governance suite."_ The defensive posture is the Pan-African / EM-fund wedge (where IBM + agentic-shift competitors are weakest) + the outcome-gate enforcement (which accelerates OUR data moat to compete with Cloverpop's). The offensive long-game is the audit-layer-for-agents pivot if/when the memo format declines.

**Update 2026-05-02 — the "shrinking middle ground" framing is partially overstated.** The 2026-05-02 agentic-shift investigation scaffolding identified three structurally protective properties of the existing product (authorship-agnostic R²F + DPR-as-contractual-artefact + structurer-accepts-arbitrary-structured-input) that mean the agentic shift widens the moat IF DI is positioned as the audit layer for high-stakes decisions regardless of input format, rather than as a memo-specific tool. R²F detectors fire identically on human-authored AND AI-authored AND agent-generated reasoning patterns. The wedge motion (human-authored memos to Individual buyers) is still the right go-to-market sequence; the path-lock decision in June 2026 establishes whether the input layer needs to expand to agent artefacts in 2026 H2 or whether that stays a Q1 2027+ reserve item.

**How to apply:** when making strategic decisions on roadmap, fundraising sequencing, or marketing positioning, evaluate against these three vectors. If a move WIDENS exposure to any of them (e.g., "let's pivot to bigger F500 CSO accounts" widens IBM exposure; "let's deprioritise the Pan-African specimen co-author motion" widens Cloverpop data-advantage exposure; "let's narrow positioning to memo-as-the-only-input-format" widens agentic-shift exposure), pause and surface the trade-off explicitly before proceeding. For Vector #3 specifically, the agentic-shift investigation in [docs/agentic-shift-investigation-q2-2026.md](docs/agentic-shift-investigation-q2-2026.md) is the primary triage instrument until the June 2026 path-lock — refer to it before any pivot conversation.

## Defensibility — the "is it just a wrapper?" answer (locked 2026-05-16, Roy-call + 2× Gemini Deep Research + master-KB synthesis)

**The honest frame (never flatter a non-moat; the founder catches flattery).** The audit engine IS a replicable prompt-wrapper — input → specialised prompts (the 12-node R²F pipeline) → output. Any competent team rebuilds it in weeks; the founder rebuilt the regulatory layer solo in days. **Do not deny this.** The company is not the engine. The company is what _accumulates around it_ that a fast-follower, an incumbent, or the model provider cannot trivially reconstruct: the enforced decision process, the tamper-evident institutional record, and the per-organisation calibration data. The wrapper is the _wedge_ that buys entry into the workflow; the accumulating decision→outcome graph + the standard the audit committee runs on is the _company_. That asset only exists once embedded — so the next 12 months are embeddedness in 1–2 orgs with measurable ROI, not more product. The rehearsable verbatim answer for advisor/investor rooms is shipped as `different_prompt_wrapper` in [killer-responses.ts](src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/data/killer-responses.ts) (KillerResponsesPlaybook, scenario `how_are_you_different`).

**The acqui-hire-vs-scale binary is FALSE at this stage** (the highest-leverage reframe; "don't let anyone box you in" applies to the advisor's framing too). The same 12-month motion — get deeply embedded in 1–2 orgs, prove measurable ROI, accumulate calibration data — is the dominant strategy under uncertainty: it maximises the acqui-hire valuation AND is the only way to discover whether the scale-company asset is real. The fork is premature optimisation; it only becomes a real decision once embeddedness is proven or not. The differentiator is _constructed by_ the embeddedness, not invented in the abstract before the wedge. Run the experiment with explicit tripwires (cannibalisation delta; calibration-latency proof; the embeddedness test) — the summer SMART goal (≥5 users + measurable ROI + a case study by ~July) IS that experiment.

**The non-wrapper vectors (every one compounds ONLY with embedded users — that is the whole point; the "pivot" is framing + sequencing, not a product rewrite).** Four core vectors, each with its highest-leverage sharpening from the master-KB synthesis:

1. **Collapse the calibration loop** (highest leverage, partly built — PriorsCaptureCard / micro-predictions / M-3 PMI auto-extract). Sharpen: force the IC to log falsifiable **90-day operational proxies at the moment of the vote** (CTO retained day-90? CRM integrated by Q2?); the Outcome Gate autonomously fires at 90 days to score them. A wrapper can't make an executive return to admit the synergy timeline was a delusion — that requires persistent embedded antagonism. **Immediately-buildable; the next ship.**
2. **Embed into the governance ritual** (the IC/board/audit-committee meeting is _run from_ the DPR, not pasted into). Sharpen: **mandatory pre-mortem dissent logging** — before a "Go" vote can be logged, the antagonist's brutal questions are surfaced and the sponsor must type a written defence into the platform. Converts read-only dashboard → mandatory write-action capital-deployment gateway. **SHIPPED 2026-05-16 (V2) — see the V2 lock below.**
3. **Cross-org Bias Genome benchmark** (the real network effect; the scale-company thesis). Sharpen: **federated toxic-combination peer-delta** — not "you have optimism bias" but "your deal teams exhibit the Sunk-Ship pattern materially more than the top quartile of peer mid-market funds"; DQI dampens/penalises against the peer baseline. Requires-scale (needs consenting competitors processing confidential deal flow).
4. **Methodology-as-standard** (R²F + DQI as the citable "FICO/GAAP of decision quality"). Sharpen: **cryptographic version-hashing into the corporate legal trail** — methodology version + SHA-256 input hashes hardcoded into the DPR; once a GC builds a 3-year audit trail on those hashes for EU AI Act Art 14 / Basel III ICAAP, switching to a cheaper wrapper means explaining to a regulator why they downgraded their evidentiary standard. Immediately-buildable (the hashing); switching cost is requires-scale.

**Three additional vectors surfaced by the master-KB synthesis:**

5. **Rigid schema enforcement (Process Power moat)** — restrict the input/workflow from an open text-box to a strict stage-gated schema (Screening → Diligence → IC Review → PMI); the longer a team works inside it the more their culture conforms, and ripping it out breaks operational alignment. Aligns with the existing Linear-style-rigid-schema lock + the conversion-mechanism directive. **SHIPPED 2026-05-16 (server-side integrity gate) — see the V5 lock below.** The _server gate_ is shipped: `validateStageTransition` is the pure SSOT for legal stage moves (committee-doc-gate ENFORCED + committee-gate cannot be skipped + backward revision kickback allowed), enforced in the container PATCH route; CommitteeReadinessGate gate-1 is now a hard gate. The _visible guided-workflow UI_ (a stage-advance control / drag board) was DELIBERATELY NOT built — there is no client stage-move surface today (read-only kanban), and adding one is net-new surface the founder explicitly deprioritised ("deepen the core flow, don't expand"). V5 is therefore a correctness/retention-foundation hardening + an honest readiness-gate truth-fix, NOT a visible workflow change yet; the guided-workflow UI is a conscious future "expand" decision, not a silent omission.
6. **Cross-decision dependency graph (Strategy Stack moat)** — extend the shipped M-7 `depends_on` ripple alert from per-pair to portfolio-wide: when a macro assumption flips ("WAEMU cycle stable"), flag every dependent deal/portfolio company simultaneously. Builds on `DecisionContainerLink`. Immediately-buildable (architecture); requires-scale to be impenetrable.
7. **Regulatory coalition lock-in (Procurement moat)** — counter-position by embedding into a model-governance incumbent's compliance wake (e.g. a Credo-AI-class partner program) as the strategic-decision tier to their model tier; the DPR maps into their Art 14 packages. The "fiduciary pincer" switching cost only materialises once GCs run regulated workflow through the system. Immediately-buildable. **Caveat: the named partner program + any peer-delta percentages are NotebookLM-surfaced hypotheses — VERIFY the partner program exists before acting; treat illustrative numbers like "42%" as do-not-quote (same discipline as Brier 0.258 / ~97% margin).**

**Forward-looking rule:** the pivot is NOT a product rewrite — it is a framing + sequencing correction. Stop positioning (and thinking of) the wrapper as the product; position the accumulating record + enforced process + standard as the product, of which the audit is the wedge. Build investment biases to Vectors 1, 5, 6 (immediately-buildable, compound with embeddedness) over feature-breadth. When a build decision drifts back toward "more audit features," check it against this lock. Full reasoning + the do-not-quote list lives in memory `project-defensibility-research-2026-05` + the master KB sources `bf1b7a7d` (V1) + `1f0b676f` (curated synthesis). Vector 1 (90-day-proxy calibration-loop deepening) — **SHIPPED 2026-05-17** (see the Vector 1 sub-lock below).

### Vector 1 — forced-at-vote 90-day operational-proxy loop (locked 2026-05-17)

**What shipped.** The founder-approved immediate next ship from the Defensibility lock, unblocked by V2. ALL container kinds (investment | acquisition | strategic — founder-scoped 2026-05-17 for full wedge-persona coverage) with an analyzed decision cannot log an outcome until ≥1 **falsifiable ≤90-day operational proxy** is on record. Pure SSOT [operational-proxy-gate.ts](src/lib/containers/operational-proxy-gate.ts) (`checkOperationalProxyGate` + `hasFalsifiable90DayProxy` + `applyProxyResolution` + `scoreResolvedProxies` + `computeProxyBrier`) is shared VERBATIM by the server hard-gate ([api/containers/[id]/outcome/route.ts](src/app/api/containers/[id]/outcome/route.ts) → 400 `OPERATIONAL_PROXY_REQUIRED`, layered right after the V2 premortem gate) and the decision-detail client guard — mirrors the V2 premortem-defence pattern exactly. 24 vitest cases ([operational-proxy-gate.test.ts](src/lib/containers/operational-proxy-gate.test.ts)). Resolution route [api/containers/[id]/proxy-resolution/route.ts](src/app/api/containers/[id]/proxy-resolution/route.ts) (owner-OR-org auth, audit `OPERATIONAL_PROXY_RESOLVED`). Surface: [OperationalProxyResolutionCard](src/components/containers/OperationalProxyResolutionCard.tsx) on the decision-detail page for all kinds when `analyzedDocCount > 0` — three states (capture-if-missing warning / resolve-when-due warning / on-record success), mirrors the V2 card shape. Day-90 cron [api/cron/proxy-resolution/route.ts](src/app/api/cron/proxy-resolution/route.ts) (in the dispatch dailyJobs after detect-outcomes): pure idempotent Brier backfill of resolved-but-unscored proxies + structured due-count log.

**Migration-free by design.** Proxies ride the existing `DecisionContainer.priors.microPredictions[]` JSON (the 2026-05-10 mechanism); `brierScore` is an additive optional field on the existing entry. No Prisma migration, no `src/lib/agents/` pipeline change. The Brier shape is the canonical PMI M-3 per-signal one verbatim (`(confidence − observed)²`, observed: true=1/partial=0.5/false=0).

**Deliberately NOT built (recorded scope boundaries, not silent omissions).** (1) **No autonomous observation inference** — the cron Brier-backfills resolved proxies but never fabricates an observation; the embedded antagonism is the _human returning_ to resolve a due proxy (surfaced on the card + the outcome gate). Auto-inference is sequenced behind this. (2) **No new Nudge type** — surfacing is the gate + the detail card; adding a `nudgeType` triggers the NUDGE_TYPE_LABELS cascade (separate subsystem) and is a recorded follow-up, not this ship. (3) **The 2026-05-10 priors-append route contract is unchanged** — the card's capture-if-missing path reuses `/api/decisions/[id]/priors` as-is (resends the existing conviction snapshot when one exists; never fabricates one), so the priors route's required-conviction lock is respected.

**Forward-looking rules:** (1) the gate predicate is the SSOT — any future surface that can log a container outcome MUST call `checkOperationalProxyGate`; never inline the rule (same discipline as the V2 `checkPremortemDefenceGate` lock). (2) When the falsifiable definition changes (horizon ceiling, min chars), edit `operational-proxy-gate.ts` only + extend the vitest suite in lockstep. (3) The "no auto-inference / no Nudge type" boundaries are load-bearing — if a future ask drifts there, route through the founder; the human-returns-to-resolve loop is the moat, not an automated score. (4) When auto-inference IS built, it extends `scoreResolvedProxies`'s input (an inferred-observation source), never replaces the human-resolution path.

### BAFTA-prep pair · FH-5.1 + FH-5.2 (locked 2026-05-17)

**What shipped.** The wrapper-rebuttal is now _true_ (V1/V2/V5 shipped, not aspirational), so the founder gets two surfaces to rehearse it before Strategy World London (T~23d). **FH-5.1** — [DefensibilityVectorsCard](src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/DefensibilityVectorsCard.tsx) on PathToHundredMillionTab (mounted after AiNativeMatrix). The honest frame + the 7 non-wrapper vectors with live `shipped/partial/next/queued` status + the acqui-hire-vs-scale-binary-is-false reframe + the do-not-quote guardrail. Resolves from the SSOT [data/defensibility-vectors.ts](src/components/founder-hub/path-to-100m/data/defensibility-vectors.ts) — the daily _visual_ reference. **FH-5.2** — three wrapper-challenge `objection_handler` scenarios in [sparring-room-data.ts](src/components/founder-hub/sparring/sparring-room-data.ts) (`preseed_vc_associate` "isn't this just a GPT wrapper" + `midmarket_corp_dev` "what stops me building it myself" + `smaller_fund_gp` "my LP will say it's ChatGPT with extra steps") — the 3-beat counter (ADMIT it's a wrapper → REFRAME wrapper=wedge vs company=accumulating record+enforced process → CLOSE on shipped embeddedness) rehearsed under pressure. The _spoken verbatim_ answer stays `different_prompt_wrapper` in killer-responses.ts; FH-5.1 is the visual ref, FH-5.2 the pressure drill, killer-responses the script.

**Forward-looking rule:** when a Defensibility vector's status changes (a `next`/`queued` ships, a new vector lands), edit `data/defensibility-vectors.ts` `DEFENSIBILITY_VECTORS` ONLY — the card + the chat-routing (founder-context.ts Defensibility block) both resolve from it; never hardcode vector status in the card. Keep `DEFENSIBILITY_VECTORS` in lockstep with the Defensibility lock's vector list + the V1/V2/V5/M-7 sub-lock statuses (same drift-class discipline as the AiNativeMatrix "every cell citable to a CLAUDE.md lock" rule). The do-not-quote set is mirrored from memory `project-defensibility-research-2026-05` — when it changes, edit both.

### V5 — rigid stage-gated decision schema · server gate (locked 2026-05-16)

**What shipped.** `validateStageTransition(input) → { allowed, reason? }` in [decision-container-modes.ts](src/lib/data/decision-container-modes.ts) is the PURE single source of truth for whether a DecisionContainer stage move is legal. Rules: (1) the committee-doc requirement is ENFORCED — a container cannot enter the committee-gate stage OR any post-committee stage unless every `requiredDocsForCommittee` type is attached (promotes CommitteeReadinessGate gate-1 from advisory to hard); (2) the committee gate cannot be SKIPPED — a pre-committee → post-committee jump is blocked even with docs present; (3) backward revision kickback + same-stage no-ops stay ALLOWED (rigidity must not block sending a decision back). Plus `getNextContainerStage(kind, stageId)`. Enforced server-side in the container PATCH route ([api/containers/[id]/route.ts](src/app/api/containers/[id]/route.ts)) — fetches attached doc types (schema-drift-tolerant: a transient join-query failure fails OPEN to the legacy id-only check, since this is a UX/integrity gate not a security/commerce boundary), calls the validator, returns 400 `STAGE_TRANSITION_BLOCKED` with the verbatim reason. 13 new vitest cases in [decision-container-modes.test.ts](src/lib/data/decision-container-modes.test.ts) (49/49 pass). CommitteeReadinessGate copy corrected to tell the truth (gate-1 hard, gates 2–5 advisory).

**What was deliberately NOT built (honest scope).** There is NO client stage-move surface today — the kanban is read-only Link cards, no drag, and no stage-select control exists anywhere. A visible "guided stage-advance workflow" / drag board is therefore net-new surface, which the founder explicitly deprioritised ("deepen the core flow, don't expand; get undeniably good at a few things"). V5 as shipped is a server-side integrity/correctness hardening + an honest readiness-gate truth-fix — it makes the rigid lifecycle TRUE for every path (API, future UI, scripts, integrations) without being a visible workflow change yet. Building the guided-workflow UI later is a conscious "expand" decision, not a silent omission. Do not re-flag the absence of a stage-advance UI as a gap — it is a recorded scope boundary.

**Cascade discipline.** `validateStageTransition` is the SSOT for stage legality — the PATCH route is the only enforcement point today; any future stage-mutation surface (a stage-advance control, a kanban drag, a bulk-move, an integration) MUST call this same pure validator client-side for guidance AND rely on the server gate, never reimplement the rules. When a 4th container mode lands (per the existing CONTAINER_MODES cascade), the validator inherits it automatically (it reads the SSOT); just extend the test suite. When the committee-doc rule changes, edit `requiredDocsForCommittee` in the SSOT only.

### V2 — mandatory pre-mortem dissent gate (locked 2026-05-16)

**What shipped.** For acquisition-mode containers with ≥1 analyzed doc, an outcome **cannot** be logged until the sponsor has recorded a substantive written defence to the Deal-Fever pre-mortem questions. The rigor goes on the tamper-evident record, not in the sponsor's head — a wrapper produces an opinion; this makes the human formally answer the antagonist. Pieces: (1) pure SSOT [premortem-defence.ts](src/lib/containers/premortem-defence.ts) — `requiresPremortemDefence` + defensive `parsePremortemDefence` + `isPremortemDefenceComplete` (every answer ≥ `MIN_DEFENCE_CHARS`) + `checkPremortemDefenceGate` (the shared verdict), 13 vitest cases, mirrors the M-7/M-3 pure-first discipline; (2) `DecisionContainer.premortemDefence Json?` (additive migration `20260516120000_container_premortem_defence`, schema-drift-tolerant, null on pre-V2 / non-acquisition rows); (3) `POST /api/containers/[id]/premortem-defence` persists the answers (acquisition-only, validates pattern + verbatim question + substantive defence, audit `PREMORTEM_DEFENCE_RECORDED`); (4) the outcome route hard-gates via the shared `checkPremortemDefenceGate` → 400 `PREMORTEM_DEFENCE_REQUIRED`; (5) [PremortemDefenceCaptureCard](src/components/containers/PremortemDefenceCaptureCard.tsx) mounted right after DealFeverPremortemCard — loads the questions from the existing deal-fever route, captures a textarea per question, flips to a success-accent read-only confirmation once complete; (6) the detail-page Log-outcome button uses the SAME pure predicate as a client guard (clear toast, never a raw 400). `premortemDefence` surfaced on `ContainerSummary`/detail (null in the list builder, like priors/culturalPairingRisk). silent-catch baseline 175 → 179 (canonical body-parse / orgId-resolve classes).

**The gate predicate is the SSOT — never reimplement.** The outcome route (server hard-gate) and the detail-page button (client guard) call the identical `checkPremortemDefenceGate`. Any future surface that can log an outcome MUST call it too; never inline the rule.

**Deliberately NOT built (recorded scope boundary, not a silent omission).** The pre-mortem defence does **not yet flow into the DPR**. `ProvenanceRecordData.reviewerDecisions` is a dormant field nothing populates and no DPR PDF page renders, and there is no container-aware DPR assembler (`assembleProvenanceRecordData` is analysis-keyed; container DPR forwards to the lead doc). Plumbing the defence into that field now would be unrendered scaffolding + a new DPR page is net-new surface — both vetoed by the founder's "deepen the core flow, don't expand, get undeniably good at a few things" filter. The defence IS already auditable (the container record + the API + the `PREMORTEM_DEFENCE_RECORDED` audit log + the visible card). **Named follow-up:** surface the recorded defence in the DPR human-oversight section once a container-aware DPR assembler exists — extend `ReviewerDecisionLog` with `premortemDefence` + populate it via an analysis→container join + render it on a HITL DPR page. Do not re-flag the DPR absence as a gap; it is this recorded boundary.

## Tech Stack

- **Framework:** Next.js 16 (App Router) + React 19 + TypeScript 5.9
- **Database:** PostgreSQL (Supabase) via Prisma 7.5
- **AI:** Google Gemini (primary), Anthropic Claude (fallback via AI_FALLBACK_ENABLED)
- **Pipeline:** LangGraph 12-node sequential+parallel agent pipeline
- **UI:** Tailwind CSS 4 + shadcn/ui + Lucide icons + Framer Motion
- **Auth:** Supabase Auth (Google OAuth)
- **Payments:** Stripe (subscriptions + per-deal audit pricing)
- **DNS + inbound email:** Cloudflare. Email Routing forwards every `*@decision-intel.com` address to the founder's personal Gmail (e.g. `security@decision-intel.com` → `folahanwilliams@gmail.com`).
- **Outbound SMTP:** Resend (`smtp.resend.com:465`, username `resend`, password = a Resend API key). Used by Supabase Auth for password-reset / magic-link / confirm emails, and by any Gmail "Send mail as" identity replying from `*@decision-intel.com`. Resend's `decision-intel.com` domain is verified with SPF + DKIM records living in Cloudflare DNS — when adding new DNS, leave those untouched.
- **Deployment:** Vercel (serverless)
- **Monitoring:** Sentry + custom AuditLog + structured logging

## Commands

```bash
npm run dev          # Start dev server (port 3000)
npm run build        # Production build (Next.js)
npm run lint         # ESLint
npm run test         # Vitest (unit tests, excludes e2e/ + voice-worker/ + all nested node_modules)
npm run slop-scan    # modem-dev/slop-scan v0.3 — second quality gate
npx playwright test  # E2E tests
npx prisma migrate dev  # Run pending migrations
npx prisma generate  # Regenerate Prisma client
```

**Pre-commit hook:** Runs four gates in order — `npm run lint:positioning` (banned-vocabulary scanner), `npm run lint:silent-catches` (silent-catch ratchet), `npm run lint:counts` (count-drift ratchet, see lock below), and `npm run audit:ai` (Gemini architectural audit). Can be bypassed with `--no-verify` but should generally be fixed instead.

**Platform audit script (on-demand 6th gate, locked 2026-05-11).** [scripts/audit-platform.mjs](scripts/audit-platform.mjs) extends the deterministic lint family with HEURISTIC checks that catch the "outdated / out of place / broken / visually incoherent" cluster — surfaced by the founder ask "is there a way for you to systematically audit and catch everything that might be outdated, out of place, broken, and visually incoherent so I don't have to keep manually going through all the pages and telling you what to fix?" Run via `npm run audit:platform` (stderr summary) or `npm run audit:platform:write` (writes markdown report to `docs/platform-audits/audit-<DATE>.md`). 9 check categories: (1) **dead-route-href** — links to retired routes (`/dashboard/playbooks`, `/dashboard/provenance`, `/dashboard/decision-log`, `/dashboard/decisions/constellation`, `/decision-alpha`, etc.); (2) **native-browser-dialog** — `window.confirm` / `window.alert` on wow-moment surfaces (with allowlist for admin/settings/founder-hub + the CLAUDE.md-named exceptions BiasCollabPanel + TeamPage); (3) **dark-mode-tailwind-token** — `text-white` / `text-gray-100..500` / `bg-zinc-800..950` / `bg-white/N` / `bg-black` on platform pages (excludes visualizations / DPR renderers / specific intentional-navy marketing surfaces / `.test.ts` files / files with `intentional-dark` header marker); (4) **hardcoded-hex-color** — `color:` / `background:` style props on platform components (allow-list for graph viz / PDF generators / canonical color maps; tolerates `#fff` and `#000`); (5) **modal-without-dialog-primitive** — `position: fixed + inset: 0 + zIndex ≥ 100` not routed through `@/components/ui/dialog`; opt-out via `intentional-modal-pattern` marker in the file header (used by QuickScanModal's intentional slide-in shape); (6) **platform-h1-token-drift** — platform-page `<h1>` using raw `text-2xl/3xl/4xl` or `fontSize: 24/28/32/36/40` instead of `var(--fs-page-h1-platform)`; (7) **stale-stage-language** — `we just launched` / `solo founder` / `early days of` / `our journey` / `just shipped` on marketing surfaces; (8) **stale-as-of-date** — `as of <Month> <Year>` more than 90 days old without `drift-tolerant` marker; (9) **deleted-component-reference** — references to retired symbols (`ContainerConstellation`, `useConstellation`, `UnifiedDecisionsFeed`, `AuditSummaryCards`, etc.). Output: 4-category report (CRITICAL · MODAL · VISUAL · STALE) with severity × rule × file:line, top 25 offenders per rule. NOT a pre-commit gate by design — it's a discovery tool the founder runs when they want to know what's stale; the dedicated lint scripts catch the deterministic drift classes at commit time. **Forward-looking rule**: when adding a new check, write a `check<Name>(files)` function returning `Finding[]` with `{ category, severity, rule, file, line, snippet, suggestion }`, wire it into `runAllChecks()`, document it in the header comment. When a check produces too many false positives, add the file/dir to the appropriate ALLOWED_PREFIXES list rather than rewriting the rule.

**Vitest exclude pattern (locked 2026-05-10).** [vitest.config.ts](vitest.config.ts) excludes `e2e/**` + `**/node_modules/**` + `voice-worker/**`. The first iteration only excluded `node_modules/**` (no glob), which **only matches the root `node_modules/`** — the voice-worker has its own nested `node_modules/` (separate Node app, Railway-hosted, NOT bundled with the Vercel main app per the voice-mode lock 2026-05-03), and vitest was recursively running upstream package tests shipped inside vendored packages (`@livekit/agents`, `pino`, `pino-pretty`, `on-exit-leak-free`). 60 "pre-existing failures" turned out to be those upstream tests failing under our vitest config — not our code. The 2026-05-10 fix: bare `node_modules/**` → `**/node_modules/**` to catch every nested location, plus `voice-worker/**` belt-and-braces to skip the whole sub-app. **Forward-looking rule**: when adding a new sub-app under `voice-worker/`-style architecture (separate Node app, own `node_modules`), add it to the vitest exclude in the same commit. The actual product test count is 713 across 53 files; if `npx vitest run` ever shows >50 failures, the first instinct should be "is the exclude pattern still right?" not "what production code broke?"

**Coverage-gap cascade + threshold ratchet (locked 2026-05-16).** A test-coverage audit found the DQI scoring engine, the R²F paper-application detectors (the IP moat), the outcome→recalibration flywheel, and the revenue/security gates almost entirely untested despite being the most procurement-load-bearing layers. Twelve new suites shipped in one cascade (122 tests, all green): **Tier 1 (pure)** `src/lib/scoring/compound-engine.test.ts` · `src/lib/scoring/weight-overrides.test.ts` · `src/lib/learning/{validity-classifier,reference-class-forecast,calibrated-rejection,decision-rubric,algorithm-aversion}.test.ts` · `src/lib/utils/redaction-scanner.test.ts`; **Tier 2/3 (Prisma-mocked)** `src/lib/learning/{recalibration,outcome-gate}.test.ts` · `src/lib/utils/{plan-limits,document-access}.test.ts`. Full suite now **1012 passing across 74 files**. **Coverage thresholds ratcheted 30 → 50/40/48/50** (stmts/branch/funcs/lines) in [vitest.config.ts](vitest.config.ts) — measured repo-wide v8 coverage at ratchet time was 53.08/43.30/51.23/53.67; floors set ~3pt below so an unrelated PR doesn't snap CI while the old silent-regress-to-30 floor is closed. **Two test-authoring lessons worth not re-deriving:** (1) **Lock actual behavior, not docstrings.** `computeConfidenceDecay`'s source comment claims sigmoid waypoints (~0.95 @ 12w) that do NOT match its `k=0.04/midpoint=40/maxDecay=0.45` implementation (real value 0.889); the regression test asserts the _real_ curve, not the aspirational comment. (2) **Vitest v4 mock-error tracking gotcha.** A `vi.fn().mockRejectedValue(...)` / `mockImplementation(() => { throw })` on a module mock fails the test EVEN WHEN application code correctly catches it (verified via instrumentation: the function returned the right permissive result + `THREW=undefined`, yet the test still failed at the mock line). The robust pattern for testing a `catch`→fallback branch: resolve the mock to an _invalid shape_ (e.g. `mockResolvedValue(null)`) so the throw originates in application code, not the mock — same branch exercised, no false failure. **Forward-looking rule**: when adding a Tier-2/3 test that must exercise a `catch` returning a fallback, drive it via an invalid resolved value, not a mock throw/reject. When coverage climbs materially (next lift = more Prisma-fixture moat-path tests), re-ratchet the floors in the same commit and update this line.

**Pre-push hook (locked 2026-04-28).** [.husky/pre-push](.husky/pre-push) runs slop-scan with a hard 4.0 trip-wire. The push is blocked if `scorePerKloc >= 4.0`. Bypass with `git push --no-verify` for audited regressions but leave a commit-msg note. The hook lives alongside the pre-commit gate so the founder doesn't have to remember to run slop-scan manually before pushing.

**Silent-catch ratchet (locked 2026-04-28; baseline drift caught 2026-05-10 deep-audit — synced from prose 155 to actual 152).** Linter at [scripts/lint-silent-catches.mjs](scripts/lint-silent-catches.mjs) scans `src/` for `.catch(arg => null/undefined/{}/[]/false/true/0/'')` and fails when the count exceeds the baseline. Actual baseline as of 2026-05-17 = **188** (the const at [scripts/lint-silent-catches.mjs](scripts/lint-silent-catches.mjs) is the source of truth — read it, do not trust this prose).
